How to request access to the Aged Care Staff Portal

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | How to request access to the Aged |
|                                   | Care Staff Portal (ACSP) + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To access the ACSP, Service       |
|                                   | Officers must have the below role |
|                                   | and resource:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The AGED CARE - SERVICE       |
|                                   |     OFFICER role (security role)  |
|                                   |     via ESSentials                |
|                                   | -   The ac_staff_portal Tivoli    |
|                                   |     Access Manager (TAM) resource |
|                                   |     via mySupport                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | How to check the security role in |
|                                   | ESSentials + Read more ...        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: all fields are optional     |
|                                   | unless marked with an asterisk.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can check if     |
|                                   | they have the security role in    |
|                                   | ESSentials by doing the           |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Open ESSentials               |
|                                   | -   Select the Access Management  |
|                                   |     tab                           |
|                                   | -   Select the Access Request     |
|                                   |     tile. The Access Request      |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   In Request Details section,   |
|                                   |     for Request For* field select |
|                                   |     ‘Self’ or ‘Other’             |
|                                   | -   Select the Existing           |
|                                   |     Assignments button underneath |
|                                   |     the User Access tab. The      |
|                                   |     Existing Assignments screen   |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do any of the existing            |
|                                   | assignments match the required    |
|                                   | AGED CARE - SERVICE OFFICER role? |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, no further action is     |
|                                   |     required in ESSentials. Go to |
|                                   |     Step 4                        |
|                                   | -   No, close the Existing        |
|                                   |     Assignments screen. Go to     |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | How to request the security role  |
|                                   | in ESSentials + Read more ...     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: all fields are optional     |
|                                   | unless marked with an asterisk.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To request the security role:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Add Role button    |
|                                   |     underneath the User Access    |
|                                   |     tab. The Select Roles pop up  |
|                                   |     box will display              |
|                                   | -   In the Functional Area field, |
|                                   |     select Aged Care from the     |
|                                   |     drop down menu                |
|                                   | -   Select the Search button. The |
|                                   |     Search results will display   |
|                                   |     in the Available assignment   |
|                                   |     block                         |
|                                   | -   Search for the required       |
|                                   |     security role and select the  |
|                                   |     row                           |
|                                   | -   Select the down arrow to move |
|                                   |     the selected role to the      |
|                                   |     Selected assignment block     |
|                                   | -   Select OK. The Access Request |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   In the Description* field,    |
|                                   |     key in the business reason    |
|                                   |     for the role request          |
|                                   | -   In the Valid From* and Valid  |
|                                   |     To* dates field, adjust the   |
|                                   |     dates if required             |
|                                   | -   Select Submit to finalise the |
|                                   |     role request                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The access request requires line  |
|                                   | manager approval, then role owner |
|                                   | approval.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once access is approved, go to    |
|                                   | Step 4.                           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | How to check if Service Officers  |
|                                   | have a P number + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must have a      |
|                                   | Tivoli Access Manager (TAM)       |
|                                   | account to access the ACSP. The   |
|                                   | Service Officer’s P number is     |
|                                   | confirmation that they have an    |
|                                   | existing TAM account.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To check the P number via the ICT |
|                                   | Security Portal (ISP):            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Open ICT Security Portal (ISP)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Copy or View Access        |
|                                   | underneath the Request Management |
|                                   | menu option                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Copy or View Access       |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the magnifying icon next   |
|                                   | to the User to View field         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Search object list screen |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key the relevant details in the   |
|                                   | search field. Note: the Search    |
|                                   | field defaults to First Name      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Search                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The search results will       |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   | -   The Agency Login ID field     |
|                                   |     displays the Service          |
|                                   |     Officer’s P number            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have a P |
|                                   | number?                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 5             |
|                                   | -   No, the Service Officer needs |
|                                   |     to complete the Medicare      |
|                                   |     Legacy Access form in         |
|                                   |     mySupport for the creation of |
|                                   |     a Tivoli Access Manager (TAM) |
|                                   |     account. Once ICT has         |
|                                   |     confirmed completion of the   |
|                                   |     TAM account, go to Step 5     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | How to request the Tivoli Access  |
|                                   | Manager (TAM) resource + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: all fields are optional     |
|                                   | unless marked with an asterisk.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To request the TAM resource:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Open mySupport                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Search field, key in       |
|                                   | ‘Medicare Access Change’. The     |
|                                   | search results will display       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Medicare Access Change |
|                                   | mySupport form. The Medicare      |
|                                   | Access Change mySupport form will |
|                                   | display                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Requested For* field,      |
|                                   | ensure the details are correct    |
|                                   | (while this defaults to the       |
|                                   | requester’s log on ID, this can   |
|                                   | change to another log on ID by    |
|                                   | selecting the drop down menu)     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the What TAM (CDMS/PDS etc.)   |
|                                   | group(s) are to be added?*        |
|                                   | section, key in the required      |
|                                   | Tivoli Access Manager (TAM)       |
|                                   | resources (ac_staff_portal).      |
|                                   | Note: valid TAM groups must be    |
|                                   | specified. Requests with invalid  |
|                                   | group(s) will not be processed    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the What additional Mainframe  |
|                                   | access is required? section, key  |
|                                   | in ‘Not applicable’               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the What TAM group(s) are to   |
|                                   | be removed? section, key in ‘Not  |
|                                   | applicable’                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the What Mainframe access is   |
|                                   | to be removed? section, key in    |
|                                   | ‘Not applicable’                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the What is the business case  |
|                                   | for this access change?* section, |
|                                   | key in the business reason:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Suggested text:               |
|                                   |     “Please add TAM account for   |
|                                   |     my [log on ID] in PRODUCTION  |
|                                   |     Environment and assign TAM    |
|                                   |     group (ac_staff_portal). This |
|                                   |     role allows me to access the  |
|                                   |     production version of the     |
|                                   |     Aged Care Staff Portal. I     |
|                                   |     require this role as part of  |
|                                   |     my job for aged care          |
|                                   |     purposes. Please do not       |
|                                   |     remove my other existing TAM  |
|                                   |     groups.”                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Submit button. The     |
|                                   | Request Details screen will       |
|                                   | display                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the User Define Request Title* |
|                                   | section, key in the title ‘Aged   |
|                                   | Care Staff Portal’                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the User Define Request        |
|                                   | Description section, key in       |
|                                   | description                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Submit                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The access request is sent to the |
|                                   | line manager for approval.        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Trouble-shooting the Aged Care Staff Portal

Table 2

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Accessing the Aged Care Staff     |
|                                   | Portal (ACSP) + Read more ...     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Access the ACSP.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the Welcome to the Aged Care   |
|                                   | Staff Portal home page screen     |
|                                   | (the ACSP home page) displayed?   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, see Table 3              |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: as ACSP uses Single Sign On |
|                                   | (SSO) access, there is no need    |
|                                   | for Service Officers to key their |
|                                   | log on ID and password.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Error message when accessing the  |
|                                   | Staff Portal + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If either error message Server    |
|                                   | was unable to fulfil the request  |
|                                   | or Unauthorised - You are not     |
|                                   | authorised to access the system   |
|                                   | displays, this is likely due to   |
|                                   | the:                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Officer not having a  |
|                                   |     Tivoli Access Manager (TAM)   |
|                                   |     group account, or             |
|                                   | -   Service Officer not having    |
|                                   |     the relevant TAM group, or    |
|                                   | -   Technical issues with the     |
|                                   |     Service Officer’s Essential   |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer’s log on |
|                                   | ID start with a P number?         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, the Service Officer needs |
|                                   |     to complete the relevant      |
|                                   |     Medicare Legacy Access form   |
|                                   |     in mySupport for the creation |
|                                   |     of a TAM group account. Once  |
|                                   |     ICT has advised the           |
|                                   |     completion of the TAM group,  |
|                                   |     the Service Officer will need |
|                                   |     to repeat Step 1 in this      |
|                                   |     table                         |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | The relevant Tivoli Access        |
|                                   | Manager (TAM) group + Read more   |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must have the    |
|                                   | relevant TAM group resource to    |
|                                   | access the Staff Portal.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | relevant TAM group resource?      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 5             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 4              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Requesting relevant TAM group +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must request the |
|                                   | relevant TAM group resource. See  |
|                                   | Step 5 in Table 1 for information |
|                                   | on how to request access.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once the TAM groups access has    |
|                                   | been granted, Service Officers    |
|                                   | must repeat Step 1 of this table. |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Checking the Service Officer’s    |
|                                   | ACMPS security role in            |
|                                   | ESSentials + Read more ...        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must check if    |
|                                   | they have the AGED CARE - SERVICE |
|                                   | OFFICER role (security role) in   |
|                                   | ESSentials. See Step 2 in Table 1 |
|                                   | for the process.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | AGED CARE - SERVICE OFFICER role? |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, no further action is     |
|                                   |     required in ESSentials. Go to |
|                                   |     Step 6                        |
|                                   | -   No, the Service Officer needs |
|                                   |     to request the security role  |
|                                   |     in ESSentials. See Table 1,   |
|                                   |     Step 3 for the process. Once  |
|                                   |     ICT has advised the           |
|                                   |     completion of the security    |
|                                   |     role, the Service Officer     |
|                                   |     will need to repeat Step 1 in |
|                                   |     this table                    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | ESSentials Technical Issues       |
|                                   | mySupport form + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers who have the     |
|                                   | required role and resource and    |
|                                   | are still unable to access the    |
|                                   | portal need to complete the       |
|                                   | ESSentials Technical Issues       |
|                                   | mySupport form. To submit the     |
|                                   | form:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Open mySupport                |
|                                   | -   In the Search field, key in   |
|                                   |     ‘ESSentials Technical         |
|                                   |     Issues’. The search results   |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   | -   Select the ESSentials         |
|                                   |     Technical Issues mySupport    |
|                                   |     form. The ESSentials          |
|                                   |     Technical Issues mySupport    |
|                                   |     form will display             |
|                                   | -   Complete all mandatory fields |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once ICT have resolved the issue, |
|                                   | the Service Officer will need to  |
|                                   | repeat Step 1 in this table       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal home page

Table 3

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Navigating the Aged Care Staff    |
|                                   | Portal (ACSP) + Read more ...     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: various menu tabs will      |
|                                   | display depending on the Service  |
|                                   | Officer's ACSP access levels.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All home and flexible care claims |
|                                   | can be approved in either ACSP or |
|                                   | Aged Care Management Payment      |
|                                   | System (ACMPS). The processing of |
|                                   | home care events can also occur   |
|                                   | in either ACSP or ACMPS. The      |
|                                   | processing of residential care    |
|                                   | events and claims must continue   |
|                                   | to occur in the System for the    |
|                                   | Payment of Aged Residential Care  |
|                                   | (SPARC). This ensures the correct |
|                                   | processing of aged care subsidies |
|                                   | and supplements for all care      |
|                                   | types. Service Officers can also  |
|                                   | use ACSP to search for services   |
|                                   | within all care types.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Access the ACSP.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Welcome to the Aged Care      |
|                                   | Staff Portal home page screen     |
|                                   | (the ACSP home page) displays the |
|                                   | following menu tabs:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   All searches - the default    |
|                                   |     option. Go to Step 2          |
|                                   | -   Care recipients - go to Step  |
|                                   |     3                             |
|                                   | -   Services - go to Step 4       |
|                                   | -   Providers - go to Step 6      |
|                                   | -   Claims - go to Step 7         |
|                                   | -   Users - go to Step 14         |
|                                   | -   Logging out of ACSP - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 15                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | All searches menu tab + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: various menu tiles display  |
|                                   | depending on the Service          |
|                                   | Officer's ACSP access levels.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the All searches menu tab,     |
|                                   | Service Officers can choose from  |
|                                   | the following menu tiles:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Care recipient search - see   |
|                                   |     Table 10, Step 2              |
|                                   | -   Service search - go to Step 5 |
|                                   | -   Provider search – see Table   |
|                                   |     5, Step 2                     |
|                                   | -   Claim search - go to Step 8   |
|                                   | -   New user request search - see |
|                                   |     Table 8, Step 6               |
|                                   | -   Logging out of ACSP - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 15                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Care recipients menu tab + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Care recipients menu tab      |
|                                   | displays the Care recipient       |
|                                   | search tile.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must select the  |
|                                   | Care recipient search tile to     |
|                                   | display the Care recipient search |
|                                   | screen.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the Care recipient search  |
|                                   | screen, see Table 10, Step 2.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To use the Services menu      |
|                                   |     tab - go to Step 4            |
|                                   | -   To use the Providers menu     |
|                                   |     tab - go to Step 6            |
|                                   | -   To use the Claims menu tab -  |
|                                   |     go to Step 7                  |
|                                   | -   To use the Users menu tab -   |
|                                   |     go to Step 14                 |
|                                   | -   To log out of the ACSP - go   |
|                                   |     to Step 15                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Services menu tab + Read more ... |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Services menu tab displays    |
|                                   | the Service search tile.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must select the  |
|                                   | Service search tile to display    |
|                                   | the Service search screen.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the Service search screen, |
|                                   | go to Step 5.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To use the Providers menu     |
|                                   |     tab - go to Step 6            |
|                                   | -   To use the Claims menu tab -  |
|                                   |     go to Step 7                  |
|                                   | -   To use the Users menu tab -   |
|                                   |     go to Step 14                 |
|                                   | -   To log out of the ACSP - go   |
|                                   |     to Step 15                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Service search screen + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can use ACSP to  |
|                                   | search for services within all    |
|                                   | care types                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All residential care events and   |
|                                   | claims must continue to occur in  |
|                                   | SPARC                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   search by a full name or      |
|                                   |     partial name when searching   |
|                                   |     by Service details            |
|                                   | -   refine their search criteria  |
|                                   |     if the 'Your search matched X |
|                                   |     services. Only 200 services   |
|                                   |     are displayed in alphabetical |
|                                   |     order below. Please refine    |
|                                   |     your search criteria if       |
|                                   |     needed' information message   |
|                                   |     displays and the relevant     |
|                                   |     service cannot be located     |
|                                   |     from the search results       |
|                                   | -   filter the search results by  |
|                                   |     the service’s operational     |
|                                   |     status to narrow the search   |
|                                   |     results                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use the Service search screen to  |
|                                   | search for an aged care service   |
|                                   | by:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   NAPS ID                       |
|                                   | -   BP ID                         |
|                                   | -   RACS ID                       |
|                                   | -   Service details               |
|                                   | -   Recent searches               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To search by NAPS ID: + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | in the Enter service details      |
|                                   | section:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select NAPS ID in the Search  |
|                                   |     by* field                     |
|                                   | -   complete the NAPS ID field -  |
|                                   |     this is a mandatory field if  |
|                                   |     the NAPS ID option has been   |
|                                   |     selected in the Search by*    |
|                                   |     field ID                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Search button          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the search results will       |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Service NAPS ID in the search     |
|                                   | results table                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the ACSP Service in Context   |
|                                   |     home page will display        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To search by BP ID: + Read more   |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | in the Enter service details      |
|                                   | section:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select BP ID in the Search    |
|                                   |     by* field                     |
|                                   | -   complete the BP ID field -    |
|                                   |     this is a mandatory field if  |
|                                   |     the BP ID option has been     |
|                                   |     selected in the Search by*    |
|                                   |     field ID                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Search button          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the search results will       |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Service NAPS ID in the search     |
|                                   | results table                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the ACSP Service in Context   |
|                                   |     home page will display        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To search by RACS ID: + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | in the Enter service details      |
|                                   | section:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select RACS ID in the Search  |
|                                   |     by* field                     |
|                                   | -   complete the RACS ID - this   |
|                                   |     is a mandatory field if the   |
|                                   |     RACS ID option has been       |
|                                   |     selected in the Search by*    |
|                                   |     field ID                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Search button          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the search results will       |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Service NAPS ID in the search     |
|                                   | results table                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the ACSP Service in Context   |
|                                   |     home page will display        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To search by Service details: +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | in the Enter service details      |
|                                   | section:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Service details in the |
|                                   |     Search by* field              |
|                                   | -   complete the Service name     |
|                                   |     field - all other fields are  |
|                                   |     optional if this field is     |
|                                   |     completed                     |
|                                   | -   complete the Care type        |
|                                   |     field - defaults to Select    |
|                                   |     all. Select the drop down     |
|                                   |     menu for Home Care,           |
|                                   |     Residential Care, Short-term  |
|                                   |     restorative care or           |
|                                   |     Transition care. All other    |
|                                   |     fields are optional if this   |
|                                   |     field is completed            |
|                                   | -   complete the Suburb field -   |
|                                   |     all other fields are optional |
|                                   |     if this field is completed    |
|                                   | -   complete the State field -    |
|                                   |     defaults to Select all.       |
|                                   |     Select the drop down menu for |
|                                   |     ACT, NSW, NT, QLD, SA, TAS,   |
|                                   |     VIC or WA - all other fields  |
|                                   |     are optional if this field is |
|                                   |     completed                     |
|                                   | -   complete the Postcode field - |
|                                   |     all other fields are optional |
|                                   |     if this field is completed    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Search button          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the search results will       |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Service NAPS ID in the search     |
|                                   | results table                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the ACSP Service in Context   |
|                                   |     home page will display        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To search by Recent searches: +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | in the Recent searches section    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Service NAPS ID in the search     |
|                                   | results table                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the ACSP Service in Context   |
|                                   |     home page will display        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | access the ACSP Service in        |
|                                   | Context home page?                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, see Table 4              |
|                                   | -   No, to log out of the ACSP,   |
|                                   |     go to Step 15                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Providers menu tab + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Providers menu tab displays   |
|                                   | the Provider search tile.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must select the  |
|                                   | Provider search tile to display   |
|                                   | the Providers search screen.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the Providers search       |
|                                   | screen, see Table 5, Step 2.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
