|                                   |     go to Step 14                 |
|                                   | -   To log out of the ACSP - go   |
|                                   |     to Step 15                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Claims menu tab + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claims for approval screen is |
|                                   | a view only screen whilst the     |
|                                   | Claim search screen is used to    |
|                                   | approve home and flexible care    |
|                                   | claims.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claims menu tab displays the  |
|                                   | following tiles:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim search - go to Step 8   |
|                                   | -   Claims for approval - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 13                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To use the Users menu tab -   |
|                                   |     go to Step 14                 |
|                                   | -   To log out of the ACSP, go to |
|                                   |     Step 15                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Claim search screen + Read more   |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claim search screen is used   |
|                                   | to search for home care and       |
|                                   | flexible care claims, regardless  |
|                                   | of their claim status.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To search for a claim, Service    |
|                                   | Officers need to:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | complete the Enter claim details  |
|                                   | section                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Search by field - defaults to |
|                                   |     Claim details                 |
|                                   | -   Claim status field - defaults |
|                                   |     to Calculated. Select the     |
|                                   |     drop down menu for Approved,  |
|                                   |     Being Approved, Being         |
|                                   |     deleted, Being refinalised,   |
|                                   |     Deleted or Select all. The    |
|                                   |     information message 'Please   |
|                                   |     complete at least one of      |
|                                   |     these fields: date from and   |
|                                   |     to, or Service ID' displays   |
|                                   |     if the Approved or Deleted    |
|                                   |     Claim status is selected      |
|                                   | -   Date type field - defaults to |
|                                   |     Finalised date                |
|                                   | -   Date from field - key the     |
|                                   |     date (DD.MM.YYYY), or select  |
|                                   |     from the calendar (select the |
|                                   |     calendar icon to display the  |
|                                   |     calendar). The date range     |
|                                   |     must be within 90 days of the |
|                                   |     Date to field                 |
|                                   | -   Date to field - key the date  |
|                                   |     (DD.MM.YYYY), or select from  |
|                                   |     the calendar (select the      |
|                                   |     calendar icon to display the  |
|                                   |     calendar). The date range     |
|                                   |     must be within 90 days of the |
|                                   |     Date from field               |
|                                   | -   Service ID type field -       |
|                                   |     defaults to NAPS ID. Select   |
|                                   |     the drop down menu for BP ID  |
|                                   | -   Service ID field              |
|                                   | -   Claim month field - select    |
|                                   |     the drop down menu for the    |
|                                   |     relevant claim month          |
|                                   | -   Claim year field - this is a  |
|                                   |     mandatory field if the Claim  |
|                                   |     month field has been          |
|                                   |     completed. Select the drop    |
|                                   |     down menu for the relevant    |
|                                   |     claim year                    |
|                                   | -   Care type field - defaults to |
|                                   |     Select all. Select the drop   |
|                                   |     down menu for Home care,      |
|                                   |     Short-term restorative care   |
|                                   |     or Transition care            |
|                                   | -   State field - defaults to     |
|                                   |     Select all. Select the drop   |
|                                   |     down menu for the relevant    |
|                                   |     State                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Search button          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the search successful?         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Claim search results      |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 9                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   For searches with a Claim     |
|                                   |     Status of Approved, Being     |
|                                   |     Approved and Being deleted,   |
|                                   |     the ‘Your search matched      |
|                                   |     <total number of claims>, but |
|                                   |     no more than 200 claims can   |
|                                   |     be displayed. The most recent |
|                                   |     200 service claims are        |
|                                   |     displayed below, please       |
|                                   |     refine your search criteria   |
|                                   |     if needed.’ message will      |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   | -   For searches with a Claim     |
|                                   |     Status of Being refinalised,  |
|                                   |     Calculated and Select all,    |
|                                   |     the ‘Your search matched      |
|                                   |     <total number of claims>, but |
|                                   |     no more than 200 claims can   |
|                                   |     be displayed. The oldest 200  |
|                                   |     service claims are displayed  |
|                                   |     below, please refine your     |
|                                   |     search criteria if needed.’   |
|                                   |     message will display          |
|                                   | -   Service Officers must refine  |
|                                   |     their search criteria         |
|                                   | -   Repeat this step (Step 8)     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: to log out of the ACSP, go  |
|                                   | to Step 15.                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Claim search results screen +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Depending on the search criteria, |
|                                   | the Claim search results screen   |
|                                   | may return:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an exact search result (that  |
|                                   |     is, claims for a single       |
|                                   |     service ID) or                |
|                                   | -   multiple search results (that |
|                                   |     is, multiple claims for       |
|                                   |     multiple service IDs)         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claim search results screen   |
|                                   | displays the following            |
|                                   | information:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service ID - Note: if Service |
|                                   |     Officers select the Service   |
|                                   |     ID hyperlink, the Service     |
|                                   |     details screen displays for   |
|                                   |     the service in context. See   |
|                                   |     Table 7, Step 2 for           |
|                                   |     information about the screen  |
|                                   | -   Service name                  |
|                                   | -   Care type                     |
|                                   | -   State                         |
|                                   | -   Finalised date                |
|                                   | -   Finalised by                  |
|                                   | -   Claim month                   |
|                                   | -   Claim ID                      |
|                                   | -   Claim type - displays the     |
|                                   |     total entitlement amounts for |
|                                   |     the current and retrospective |
|                                   |     claim months                  |
|                                   | -   Total entitlements            |
|                                   | -   Status - Note: only claims    |
|                                   |     with Calculated status can be |
|                                   |     approved in the ACSP          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the claim status Calculated?   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Calculated         |
|                                   |     hyperlink for the relevant    |
|                                   |     service ID                    |
|                                   | -   The Claim entitlements screen |
|                                   |     for approval will display     |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 11                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The claim status is           |
|                                   |     Refinalised                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Refinalisation     |
|                                   |     required hyperlink for the    |
|                                   |     relevant service ID           |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 10                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: to log out of the ACSP, go  |
|                                   | to Step 15                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 10                                | Claim entitlements screen for     |
|                                   | refinalisation + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Restricted access is required to  |
|                                   | perform the Refinalisation        |
|                                   | function in ACSP.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claim entitlements screen     |
|                                   | displays the following            |
|                                   | information:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service ID - Note: if Service |
|                                   |     Officers selects the Service  |
|                                   |     ID hyperlink, the Service     |
|                                   |     details screen displays for   |
|                                   |     the service in context. See   |
|                                   |     Table 7 Step 2 for details    |
|                                   |     about the screen              |
|                                   | -   Service name                  |
|                                   | -   Care type                     |
|                                   | -   State                         |
|                                   | -   Finalised date                |
|                                   | -   Finalised by                  |
|                                   | -   Claim month                   |
|                                   | -   Claim ID                      |
|                                   | -   Claim type                    |
|                                   | -   Total entitlements - displays |
|                                   |     the total entitlement for the |
|                                   |     current and retrospective     |
|                                   |     claim month(s)                |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | Refinalise the claim?             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Refinalise claim   |
|                                   |     button                        |
|                                   | -   The message ‘SUCCESS: The     |
|                                   |     claim refinalisation for the  |
|                                   |     service is being processed’   |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   | -   The claim status will update  |
|                                   |     to Being refinalised          |
|                                   | -   The claim status will be      |
|                                   |     updated to Calculated after   |
|                                   |     the Refinalisation process is |
|                                   |     complete                      |
|                                   | -   A different Service Officer   |
|                                   |     to the one who refinalised    |
|                                   |     the claim can progress the    |
|                                   |     claim approval process        |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 8 for the Claim    |
|                                   |     Search screen                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Delete all button  |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 12                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 11                                | Claim entitlements screen for     |
|                                   | approval + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Restricted access is required to  |
|                                   | perform the Approve and/or Delete |
|                                   | claim functionality in ACSP. Only |
|                                   | a Service Officer different to    |
|                                   | the one who finalised or          |
|                                   | refinalised the claim can approve |
|                                   | the claim.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   must review each claim’s      |
|                                   |     entitlement information prior |
|                                   |     to the claim approval or      |
|                                   |     claim deletion                |
|                                   | -   can use the Payments          |
|                                   |     Additions screen in ACMPS to  |
|                                   |     investigate claim             |
|                                   |     entitlements. See the Search  |
|                                   |     and view claims table in      |
|                                   |     Maintain claims in Aged Care  |
|                                   |     Management Payment System     |
|                                   |     (ACMPS) for the process       |
|                                   | -   can also use the Claim        |
|                                   |     approvals functionality in    |
|                                   |     ACMPS to approve or delete    |
|                                   |     claims                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claim entitlements screen     |
|                                   | displays the following            |
|                                   | information:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service ID - Note: if Service |
|                                   |     Officers selects the Service  |
|                                   |     ID hyperlink, the Service     |
|                                   |     details screen displays for   |
|                                   |     the service in context. See   |
|                                   |     Table 7, Step 2 for details   |
|                                   |     about the screen              |
|                                   | -   Service name                  |
|                                   | -   Care type                     |
|                                   | -   State                         |
|                                   | -   Finalised date                |
|                                   | -   Finalised by                  |
|                                   | -   Claim month                   |
|                                   | -   Claim ID                      |
|                                   | -   Claim type                    |
|                                   | -   Total entitlements - displays |
|                                   |     the total entitlement for the |
|                                   |     current and retrospective     |
|                                   |     claim month(s)                |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Prior to claim approval or claim  |
|                                   | deletion, Service Officers must:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   review each claim’s           |
|                                   |     entitlement information       |
|                                   | -   use the Payments Additions    |
|                                   |     screen in ACMPS to            |
|                                   |     investigate claim             |
|                                   |     entitlements. See the Search  |
|                                   |     and view claims table in      |
|                                   |     Maintain claims in Aged Care  |
|                                   |     Management Payment System     |
|                                   |     (ACMPS)                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | approve the claim(s)?             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Approve claim          |
|                                   | -   The message ‘SUCCESS: The     |
|                                   |     claim approval for the        |
|                                   |     service is being processed.’  |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   | -   The Status for the relevant   |
|                                   |     claim and associated          |
|                                   |     retrospective claims will     |
|                                   |     display as Being Approved     |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, Service Officers can either   |
|                                   | select:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Delete all to delete the      |
|                                   |     relevant claim and associated |
|                                   |     retrospective claims. Go to   |
|                                   |     Step 12                       |
|                                   | -   Go to the list of claims to   |
|                                   |     return to the Claim search    |
|                                   |     results screen. The claims    |
|                                   |     status and associated claims  |
|                                   |     status for the relevant       |
|                                   |     service ID remains as         |
|                                   |     Calculated (the claims have   |
|                                   |     not been approved)            |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: to log out of the ACSP, go  |
|                                   | to Step 15                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 12                                | Deleting the claims + Read more   |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | By deleting the relevant claim,   |
|                                   | Service Officers will also be     |
|                                   | deleting all associated           |
|                                   | retrospective claims. To delete   |
|                                   | the current and retrospective     |
|                                   | claims:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Delete all                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The message ‘You are about to |
|                                   |     Delete the claims for the     |
|                                   |     service. All associated retro |
|                                   |     claims for the service will   |
|                                   |     also be deleted. Are you sure |
|                                   |     you want to delete the        |
|                                   |     claim?’ will display          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes to continue            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The message ‘SUCCESS: The     |
|                                   |     claim deletion for the        |
|                                   |     service is being processed’   |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Status for the current and    |
|                                   | retrospective claims will display |
|                                   | as Being deleted                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: to log out of the ACSP, go  |
|                                   | to Step 15                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 13                                | Claims for approval screen + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claims for approval screen is |
|                                   | a view only screen. The screen    |
|                                   | lists all the home care and       |
|                                   | flexible care claims ready for    |
|                                   | approval.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: all home care and flexible  |
|                                   | care claim approvals can also     |
|                                   | occur in ACMPS. See Maintain      |
|                                   | Claims in the Aged Care           |
|                                   | Management Payment System (ACMPS) |
|                                   | for the approval process.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claims for approval screen    |
|                                   | displays:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service ID - if Service       |
|                                   |     Officers selects the Service  |
|                                   |     ID hyperlink, the Service     |
|                                   |     details screen displays for   |
|                                   |     the service in context. See   |
|                                   |     Table 7, Step 2 for           |
|                                   |     information about the screen  |
|                                   | -   Service name                  |
|                                   | -   Care type                     |
|                                   | -   State                         |
|                                   | -   Finalised date - defaults to  |
|                                   |     ascending order               |
|                                   | -   Finalised by                  |
|                                   | -   Claim month                   |
|                                   | -   Claim ID                      |
|                                   | -   Claim type                    |
|                                   | -   Total entitlements - displays |
|                                   |     the current claim’s           |
|                                   |     entitlement amount and if     |
|                                   |     applicable, any retrospective |
|                                   |     claims’ entitlement amounts.  |
|                                   |     Note: retrospective claims’   |
|                                   |     entitlement amounts will      |
|                                   |     display as a single total     |
|                                   |     amount                        |
|                                   | -   Status - only displays the    |
|                                   |     Calculated status             |
|                                   | -   Legend - displays the         |
|                                   |     definition of the various     |
|                                   |     care types                    |
|                                   | -   Filter by - Service Officers  |
|                                   |     can filter the list by the    |
|                                   |     service name                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To use the Users menu tab -   |
|                                   |     go to Step 14                 |
|                                   | -   To log out of the ACSP, go to |
|                                   |     Step 15                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 14                                | Users menu tab + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The New user request search   |

| 15                                | Logging out of the ACSP + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To log out of the ACSP, Service   |
|                                   | Officers need to:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Logout button at   |
|                                   |     the top far right corner of   |
|                                   |     the screen                    |
|                                   | -   the Log out? pop up           |
|                                   |     notification displays         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Log out? pop up            |
|                                   | notification, Service Officers    |
|                                   | can select:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes - Logs the Service        |
|                                   |     Officer out of the ACSP. The  |
|                                   |     Intranet home page displays   |
|                                   | -   No - Returns the Service      |
|                                   |     Officer to the ACSP           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the ACSP is idle for 25    |
|                                   |     minutes a pop up notification |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   | -   The pop up notification       |
|                                   |     advises the session will      |
|                                   |     expire if a selection is not  |
|                                   |     made and the displayed        |
|                                   |     counter counts down           |

Aged Care Staff Portal Service in Context home page key features

Table 4

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP)     |
|                                   | Service in Context home page +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: all home and flexible care  |
|                                   | claims can be approved in either  |
|                                   | ACSP or Aged Care Management      |
|                                   | Payment System (ACMPS). The       |
|                                   | processing of home care events    |
|                                   | can also occur in either ACSP or  |
|                                   | ACMPS. The processing of          |
|                                   | residential care events and       |
|                                   | claims must continue to occur in  |
|                                   | the System for the Payment of     |
|                                   | Aged Residential Care (SPARC).    |
|                                   | This ensures the correct          |
|                                   | processing of aged care subsidies |
|                                   | and supplements for all care      |
|                                   | types. Service Officers can also  |
|                                   | use ACSP to search for services   |
|                                   | within all care types.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ACSP Service in Context home  |
|                                   | page provides quick access to the |
|                                   | most frequently used screens. The |
|                                   | ACSP Service home page only       |
|                                   | displays for the service in       |
|                                   | context, e.g. displays the        |
|                                   | selected service’s details.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key features of the ACSP Service  |
|                                   | in Context home page are the:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Main menu (Hamburger          |
|                                   |     button) - go to Step 2        |
|                                   | -   Quick find search bar - go to |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
|                                   | -   Quick link navigation bar -   |
|                                   |     go to Step 4                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Main menu (Hamburger button) +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, select the icon from   |
|                                   | the top left corner of the screen |
|                                   | to access the Main menu.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The menu contains the below       |
|                                   | sections:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Staff Portal        |
|                                   | -   Service                       |
|                                   | -   Service management            |
|                                   | -   Claims                        |
|                                   | -   Payment statements            |
|                                   | -   Reports                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An extended menu (additional      |
|                                   | options) display to Service       |
|                                   | Officers:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   depending on the service      |
|                                   |     selected, or                  |
|                                   | -   when viewing care recipient   |
|                                   |     details and/or submitting     |
|                                   |     events at the care recipient  |
|                                   |     level                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Quick find search bar, go to  |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
|                                   | -   Quick link navigation bar, go |
|                                   |     to Step 4                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Quick find search bar + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the Quick find search bar   |
|                                   | cannot be used to search for      |
|                                   | individual care recipients.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use the Quick find search bar to  |
|                                   | quickly access a specific screen. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, the Quick find search  |
|                                   | bar is located underneath the     |
|                                   | Welcome to the Aged Care Staff    |
|                                   | Portal banner.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Type the name of the screen in    |
|                                   | the search bar. A drop down list  |
|                                   | appears showing the names of all  |
|                                   | screens containing those          |
|                                   | keyword(s).                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the Quick link navigation  |
|                                   | bar, go to Step 4.                |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Quick links navigation bar + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Quick links navigation bar    |
|                                   | displays a list of frequently     |
|                                   | used screens. The Quick links     |
|                                   | navigation bar is located on the  |
|                                   | left hand side of the ACSP        |
|                                   | Service in Context home page.     |

| 3                                 | Using the Provider search         |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can use the      |
|                                   | Provider search screen to search  |
|                                   | for active and inactive providers |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   search by a full name or      |
|                                   |     partial name when searching   |
|                                   |     by Provider details           |
|                                   | -   select Clear to clear the     |
|                                   |     search criteria               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers may need to      |
|                                   | refine their search criteria if   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Your search matched X     |
|                                   |     providers. Only 200 providers |
|                                   |     are displayed in alphabetical |
|                                   |     order below. Please refine    |
|                                   |     your search criteria if       |
|                                   |     needed information message    |
|                                   |     displays and they cannot      |
|                                   |     locate the relevant provider  |
|                                   |     from the search results       |
|                                   | -   the No results information    |
|                                   |     message displays              |

|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |

|                                   | provider by selecting either:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Search by NAPS ID - default       |
|                                   | option                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key in the NAPS ID in the     |
|                                   |     NAPS ID field                 |
|                                   | -   Select Search                 |
|                                   | -   The Provider details screen   |
|                                   |     for the relevant provider     |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Search by BP ID - select the drop |
|                                   | down menu to display this search  |
|                                   | option                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key in the BP ID in the BP ID |
|                                   |     field                         |
|                                   | -   Select Search                 |
|                                   | -   The Provider details screen   |
|                                   |     for the relevant provider     |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Search by Provider details -      |
|                                   | select the drop down menu to      |
|                                   | display this search option        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key in the Provider name in   |
|                                   |     the Provider name field. This |
|                                   |     is a free text field and all  |
|                                   |     other fields are optional if  |
|                                   |     this field is completed       |
|                                   | -   Key in the ABN in the ABN     |
|                                   |     field. This field only allows |
|                                   |     numerical values and all      |
|                                   |     other fields are optional if  |
|                                   |     this field is completed       |
|                                   | -   Key in the Suburb in the      |
|                                   |     Suburb field. All other       |
|                                   |     fields are optional if this   |
|                                   |     field is completed            |
|                                   | -   Select the relevant State     |
|                                   |     from the drop down menu in    |
|                                   |     the State field. All other    |
|                                   |     fields are optional if this   |
|                                   |     field is completed            |
|                                   | -   Key in the Postcode in the    |
|                                   |     Postcode field. This field    |
|                                   |     only allows numerical values  |
|                                   |     and all other fields are      |
|                                   |     optional if this field is     |
|                                   |     completed                     |
|                                   | -   Select Search                 |
|                                   | -   The Provider search results   |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   Select the relevant           |
|                                   |     hyperlinked Providers NAPS ID |
|                                   |     in the search results table   |
|                                   | -   The Provider details screen   |
|                                   |     for the selected provider     |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Search by Recent searches in the  |
|                                   | Recent searches section           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the relevant           |
|                                   |     hyperlinked Providers NAPS ID |
|                                   |     in the search results table   |
|                                   | -   The Provider details screen   |
|                                   |     for the selected provider     |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Provider search results    |
|                                   | screen, Service Officers can also |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | type in a keyword in the Search   |
|                                   | bar to search for all records     |
|                                   | that contain the keyword          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | filter the search results by the  |
|                                   | provider’s operational status to  |
|                                   | narrow the search results         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | sort the search results in        |
|                                   | alphabetical order by Provider    |
|                                   | name                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the number of records to   |
|                                   | display from the Show records     |
|                                   | drop down list (bottom left       |
|                                   | corner of the screen)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | go to a different page by         |
|                                   | selecting either:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   First, Previous, Next or Last |
|                                   |     options, or                   |
|                                   | -   the relevant page number      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Back to search to return   |
|                                   | to the Provider search screen     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

|                                   |     keyword                       |
|                                   |     Note: search results display  |
|                                   |     where the keyword is used     |
|                                   |     anywhere on the record, even  |
|                                   |     if it appears in the middle   |
|                                   |     of another word               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Legend button to       |
|                                   | display code explanations         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | view the                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   care recipient’s personal     |
|                                   |     details under the Care        |
|                                   |     recipient heading (care       |
|                                   |     recipient ID, family name and |
|                                   |     given name)                   |
|                                   | -   Functional capacity score     |
|                                   |     (MBI) - displays for flexible |
|                                   |     care services only            |
|                                   | -   Care setting days - displays  |
|                                   |     for flexible care services    |
|                                   |     only                          |
|                                   | -   Event details under the       |
|                                   |     Events heading (entry,        |
|                                   |     departures and leave details  |
|                                   |     etc.)                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | view the events by Status type:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   All                           |
|                                   | -   Accepted                      |
|                                   | -   Deleted                       |
|                                   | -   Held                          |
|                                   | -   Rejected                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the number of records to   |
|                                   | display from the Show records     |
|                                   | drop down list (bottom left       |
|                                   | corner of the screen)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | go to a different page by         |
|                                   | selecting either the:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   First, Previous, Next or Last |
|                                   |     options, or                   |
|                                   | -   the relevant page number      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | finalise the current claim        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Finalise the current claim + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a claim submits successfully,  |
|                                   | a successful message displays     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An error message displays if      |
|                                   | there is an issue with the claim  |
|                                   | finalisation process              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Entry events with a Held status   |
|                                   | will not be processed as part of  |
|                                   | the current claim’s finalisation  |
|                                   | process and may result in over    |
|                                   | occupancy issues                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These entry events are due to a   |
|                                   | known timing issue with over      |
|                                   | lapping periods of care. That is, |
|                                   | the care recipient has entered    |
|                                   | into care of the new aged care    |
|                                   | service but a departure event has |
|                                   | not been submitted by the         |
|                                   | previous aged care service        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These entry events are resolved   |
|                                   | when Services Australia has       |
|                                   | received the departure event from |
|                                   | the previous aged care service    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The over occupancy report message |
|                                   | and report displays after         |
|                                   | submitting the claim if the       |
|                                   | service is over occupied          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The over occupancy issue must be  |
|                                   | resolved before the claim can be  |
|                                   | resubmitted                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To assist in resolving the over   |
|                                   | occupancy issue, Service Officers |
|                                   | can select the Over occupancy     |
|                                   | report option to identify:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the specific care recipients  |
|                                   |     causing the over occupancy    |
|                                   | -   the number of approved places |
|                                   |     over occupied (the number of  |
|                                   |     care recipients over          |
|                                   |     occupied)                     |
|                                   | -   total occupancy               |
|                                   | -   approved occupancy            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Current claim screen,      |
|                                   | Service Officers can finalise the |
|                                   | current claim by selecting the    |
|                                   | Finalise claim button.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A warning message displays:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | ‘WARNING: The claim may contain   |
|                                   | outstanding events with a status  |
|                                   | of being processed or held and    |
|                                   | may or may not be subsequently    |
|                                   | accepted and included within this |
|                                   | claim for payment. Do you want to |
|                                   | finalise the claim for [month     |
|                                   | year] with these events           |
|                                   | outstanding?’                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can select:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, to finalise the claim        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit to finalise the |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, to cancel the claim           |
|                                   | finalisation process              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Current claim screen will |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Going to the All service claims   |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use the All service claims screen |
|                                   | to view and/or check the status   |
|                                   | of all claims (current and        |
|                                   | historical claims) for the        |
|                                   | service in context.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the ACSP Service in Context    |
|                                   | home page, go to the All service  |
|                                   | claims screen using any of the    |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the Main menu (Hamburger button)  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Main menu          |
|                                   | -   select All service claims     |
|                                   |     under the Claims section      |
|                                   | -   the All service claims screen |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the Quick find navigation bar     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   type All service claims in    |
|                                   |     the Quick find search bar     |
|                                   | -   select Go                     |
|                                   | -   the All service claims screen |
|                                   |     displays                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Using the All service claims      |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The All service claims screen,    |
|                                   | displays the claim history in the |
|                                   | below table format:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim month - select the up   |
|                                   |     or down arrows to display the |
|                                   |     months in ascending or        |
|                                   |     descending order              |
|                                   | -   Date finalised - select the   |
|                                   |     up or down arrows to display  |
|                                   |     the dates in ascending or     |
|                                   |     descending order              |
|                                   | -   Authorised person - select    |
|                                   |     the up or down arrows to      |
|                                   |     display the authorised        |
|                                   |     person’s name in alphabetical |
|                                   |     order                         |
|                                   | -   Channel - Services Australia  |
|                                   |     (Service Officers) or the     |
|                                   |     Portal (the aged care         |
|                                   |     service). Select the up or    |
|                                   |     down arrows to display the    |
|                                   |     Channel form in alphabetical  |
|                                   |     order                         |
|                                   | -   Date approved - select the up |
|                                   |     or down arrows to display the |
|                                   |     dates in ascending or         |
|                                   |     descending order              |
|                                   | -   Status - Approved, Open or    |
|                                   |     Processing. Select the up or  |
|                                   |     down arrows to display the    |
|                                   |     Status type in alphabetical   |
|                                   |     order                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | search for a specific or current  |
|                                   | claim                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   type in a keyword in the      |
|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword                       |
|                                   |     Note: search results display  |
|                                   |     where the keyword is used     |
|                                   |     anywhere on the record, even  |
|                                   |     if it appears in the middle   |
|                                   |     of another word               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | change the claim year             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the year from the      |
|                                   |     Claims for year drop down     |
|                                   |     list. Note: the Claims for    |
|                                   |     year defaults to the current  |
|                                   |     year                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the number of records      |
|                                   | display from the Show records     |
|                                   | drop down list (bottom left       |
|                                   | corner of the screen)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | go to a different page by         |
|                                   | selecting either the:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   First, Previous, Next or Last |
|                                   |     options, or                   |
|                                   | -   the relevant page number      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

| 9                                 | Using the Service payment summary |

|                                   |     displays are dependent on the |
|                                   |     service in context’s care     |
|                                   |     type e.g. Dementia supplement |
|                                   |     displays only for home care   |
|                                   |     purposes                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Adjustments for current       |
|                                   | period section                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Commonwealth unspent amount   |
|                                   |     (for home care only)          |
|                                   | -   Means tested subsidy          |
|                                   |     reduction (for home care      |
|                                   |     only)                         |
|                                   | -   Means tested subsidy review   |
|                                   |     refund (for home care only)   |
|                                   | -   Manual adjustments            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Adjustments for previous      |
|                                   | periods section                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Displays for all care types   |
|                                   | -   The supplements displays in   |
|                                   |     this section are dependent on |
|                                   |     the service in context’s care |
|                                   |     type e.g. dementia supplement |
|                                   |     displays only for home care   |
|                                   |     purposes                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Outstanding balance and       |
|                                   | advance section                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Total subsidy paid                |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | (previous claim period)           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Less Advance (for flexible care   |
|                                   | services only)                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Less Ad-hoc payment (for home     |
|                                   | care services only)               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Total amount paid to the provider |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For home care services only       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Income tested subsidy review  |
|                                   |     refund                        |
|                                   | -   Income test reduction         |
|                                   | -   CW Unspent amounts            |
|                                   | -   Payment Due/Payment Held over |
|                                   |     amount                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the Service payment summary  |
|                                   | screen, Service Officers can:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | change the Claim month            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the month from the     |
|                                   |     Claim month drop down list    |
|                                   |     Note: the Claim month         |
|                                   |     defaults to the current       |
|                                   |     payment statement             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | download the payment statement in |
|                                   | CSV, XML or PDF format            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the relevant format    |
|                                   |     button                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | view historical payment           |
|                                   | statements that were finalised    |
|                                   |                                   |

Table 7

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
