| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: all home and flexible care  |
|                                   | claims can be approved in either  |
|                                   | ACSP or Aged Care Management      |
|                                   | Payment System (ACMPS). The       |
|                                   | processing of home care events    |
|                                   | can also occur in either ACSP or  |
|                                   | ACMPS. The processing of          |
|                                   | residential care events and       |
|                                   | claims must continue to occur in  |
|                                   | the System for the Payment of     |
|                                   | Aged Residential Care (SPARC).    |
|                                   | This ensures the correct          |
|                                   | processing of aged care subsidies |
|                                   | and supplements for all care      |
|                                   | types. Service Officers can also  |
|                                   | use ACSP to search for services   |
|                                   | within all care types.            |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service details                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 2                        |
|                                   | -   Viewing the screen, go to     |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service contact details           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 4                        |
|                                   | -   Viewing the screen, go to     |
|                                   |     Step 5                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service approved places           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |

|                                   |     Step 12                       |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     Step 13                       |

|                                   |     contacts - go to Step 10      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Register new service contact      |
|                                   | details + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: The information message     |
|                                   | ‘There is no contact registered   |
|                                   | for this service. Please register |
|                                   | a contact.’ will display if there |
|                                   | are no service contact details    |
|                                   | registered for the service.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are mandatory.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Service contact screen, to |

|                                   | -   complete the Given name field |
|                                   | -   complete the Primary phone    |
|                                   |     number field                  |
|                                   | -   complete the Email address    |
|                                   |     field                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete the Register new service |
|                                   | contact details process?          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 7                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     display asking the Service    |
|                                   |     Officers to select Yes or No  |
|                                   |     to cancel the process         |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The Service user summary      |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |

|                                   |     status to View bank details   |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     (bottom left corner of the    |
|                                   |     screen)                       |

|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword. Search results       |
|                                   |     display where the keyword is  |
|                                   |     used anywhere on the record,  |
|                                   |     even if it appears in the     |
|                                   |     middle of another word        |
|                                   | -   select the relevant           |
|                                   |     hyperlinked bank details      |

|                                   |     i.e. the date the advance was |
|                                   |     approved                      |
|                                   | -   Advance amount paid           |
|                                   | -   Claim’s certification date,   |
|                                   |     i.e. the date the claim was   |
|                                   |     approved                      |
|                                   | -   Payment held over, i.e. any   |
|                                   |     amount the service owes to    |
|                                   |     Services Australia            |
|                                   | -   Claim amount paid             |
|                                   | -   Total amount paid             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To download the financial year    |
|                                   | payments report, select the CSV   |
|                                   | button.                           |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage service user details

Table 8

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Manage service users      |
|                                   |     screen is only available to   |
|                                   |     Service Officers when they    |
|                                   |     are using the Service in      |
|                                   |     Context view                  |
|                                   | -   The User search screen is     |
|                                   |     only available to Service     |
|                                   |     Officers when they are using  |
|                                   |     the Care Recipient in Context |
|                                   |     (CRiC) view                   |
|                                   | -   The New user request search   |
|                                   |     screen is available to        |
|                                   |     Service Officers when they    |
|                                   |     are using both the Service in |
|                                   |     Context and CRiC views        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To manage service user details,   |
|                                   | Service Officers can choose from  |
|                                   | the following menu options:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manage service user details       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 2                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     3                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | User search                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 4                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     5                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | New user request search           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 6                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     7                             |

|                                   | view.                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Manage service user details   |
|                                   | screen displays the ‘A users’ who |
|                                   | are associated with the service   |
|                                   | in context. Service Officers can  |
|                                   | use the Manage service user       |
|                                   | details screen to:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   search for ‘A users’          |
|                                   | -   amend existing ‘A users’      |
|                                   |     personal information and      |
|                                   | -   amend or end date existing ‘A |
|                                   |     users’ access levels          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Manage service users screen   |
|                                   | displays the following fields:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   User details - details the ‘A |
|                                   |     users’ personal information   |
|                                   | -   User access dates - details   |
|                                   |     the start dates and end dates |
|                                   |     of the ‘A users’ access       |
|                                   | -   User access levels - details  |
|                                   |     the ‘A users’ access levels   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To amend existing ‘A users’       |
|                                   | personal information and access   |
|                                   | levels, see the New user          |
|                                   | registration process via the      |
|                                   | manual channel Table in Online    |
|                                   | claiming registration process for |
|                                   | aged care providers.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Going to the User search screen + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the User search screen is   |
|                                   | only available to Service         |
|                                   | Officers when they are using the  |
|                                   | Care Recipient in Context (CRiC)  |
|                                   | view.                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, go to the Manage user  |
|                                   | details screen using any of the   |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   select User search under the  |
|                                   |     Aged Care Staff Portal        |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   the User search screen        |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick find navigation bar         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   type User search in the Quick |
|                                   |     find search bar               |
|                                   | -   select Go                     |
|                                   | -   the User search screen        |
|                                   |     displays                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Using the User search screen +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | There are 2 channels of receiving |
|                                   | new ‘A users’ requests:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   online (Aged Care Provider    |
|                                   |     Portal (ACPP)) and            |
|                                   | -   manual (the                   |
|                                   |     Register, amend or remove     |
|                                   |     users for Aged Care Provider  |
|                                   |     Portal form (AC004) form)     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The User search screen is only    |
|                                   | applicable for the new user       |
|                                   | requests via the manual channel   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For the online new user requests  |
|                                   | process, see Step 6               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The User search screen is only    |
|                                   | available to Service Officers     |
|                                   | when they are using the Care      |
|                                   | Recipient in Context (CRiC) view  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The User search screen displays   |
|                                   | the ‘A users’ who are associated  |
|                                   | with the service in context.      |
|                                   | Service Officers can use the User |
|                                   | search screen to:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   search for ‘A users’          |
|                                   | -   amend existing ‘A users’      |
|                                   |     personal information          |
|                                   | -   amend or end date existing ‘A |
|                                   |     users’ access levels, and     |
|                                   | -   register new ‘A users’ to     |
|                                   |     process new user requests     |
|                                   |     received via the manual       |
|                                   |     channel                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the User search screen,        |
|                                   | Service Officers can search for   |
|                                   | the ‘A users’ by selecting either |
|                                   | the:                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | User ID - default option          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   key in ‘A number’ in the User |
|                                   |     ID field                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | User details                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   key the family name in the    |
|                                   |     Family name field. Note: this |
|                                   |     must be a full name search    |
|                                   | -   key the given name in the     |
|                                   |     Given name field. Note: this  |
|                                   |     must be a full name search    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Search button to       |
|                                   | display the search results.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To amend existing ‘A users’       |
|                                   | personal information and access   |
|                                   | levels, see the New user          |
|                                   | registration process via the      |
|                                   | manual channel Table in Online    |
|                                   | claiming registration process for |
|                                   | aged care providers.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To register new ‘A users’, see    |
|                                   | Step 3 of the New user            |
|                                   | registration process via the      |
|                                   | manual channel Table in Online    |
|                                   | claiming registration process for |
|                                   | aged care providers.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | -   the New user request search   |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Using the New user request search |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | There are 2 channels of receiving |
|                                   | a new ‘A users’ requests:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Online (ACPP), and            |
|                                   | -   Manual (the Register, amend   |
|                                   |     or remove users for Aged Care |
|                                   |     Provider Portal form (AC004)  |
|                                   |     form)                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The New user request search       |
|                                   | screen is applicable for online   |
|                                   | new user requests submitted via   |
|                                   | the ACPP                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Step 5 for the manual new     |
|                                   | user requests process             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The New user request search       |
|                                   | screen is available to Services   |
|                                   | Officers when they are using both |
|                                   | the Service in Context and CRiC   |
|                                   | views                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional, unless   |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the New user request search    |
|                                   | screen, Service Officers can      |
|                                   | search for a specific new user    |
|                                   | request by selecting either:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Search by Request ID - default    |
|                                   | option                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   key in the ‘Request ID’ in    |
|                                   |     the Request ID* field         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Search by User details            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   key the family name in the    |
|                                   |     Family name* field            |
|                                   | -   key the given name in the     |
|                                   |     Given name field              |
|                                   | -   key the phone number in the   |
|                                   |     Primary phone number field    |
|                                   |     (if known)                    |
|                                   | -   key the email address in the  |
|                                   |     Email field (if known)        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Search button.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the search successful?         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   For an exact matched search   |
|                                   |     result, go to Step 8          |
|                                   | -   For multiple search results,  |
|                                   |     go to Step 9                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the information message No    |
|                                   |     records available. Please     |
|                                   |     check the search terms and    |
|                                   |     try again will display for    |
|                                   |     unsuccessful searches         |
|                                   | -   select Clear to clear the     |
|                                   |     search parameters. Repeat     |
|                                   |     this step (Step 7)            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Exact matched search results +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An exact matched search result    |
|                                   | displays the following            |
|                                   | information:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Request ID                    |
|                                   | -   User ID                       |
|                                   | -   Family name                   |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Primary phone number          |
|                                   | -   Secondary phone number        |
|                                   | -   Email address                 |
|                                   | -   Service details               |
|                                   | -   Access level                  |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 10.                    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Multiple search results + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Multiple search results displays  |
|                                   | in the following table format:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Request ID - Service Officers |
|                                   |     can select the new user       |
|                                   |     request hyperlink in the      |
|                                   |     Request ID column             |
|                                   | -   User ID                       |
|                                   | -   Family name                   |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Requested by - details the ID |
|                                   |     of the ‘A user’ with the      |
|                                   |     organisation administrator    |
|                                   |     access who submitted the new  |
|                                   |     user request via the ACPP     |
|                                   | -   Date requested                |
|                                   | -   Approved by/Rejected by -     |
|                                   |     details the log on ID of the  |
|                                   |     Service Officer who approved  |
|                                   |     or rejected the new user      |
|                                   |     request                       |
|                                   | -   Date approved/Rejected        |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the new user request       |
|                                   | hyperlink in the Request ID       |
|                                   | column to display the details of  |
|                                   | a specific request                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | type in a keyword in the Search   |
|                                   | bar to search for all records     |
|                                   | that contain the keyword          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | view the events by Status type:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Status type can either be |
|                                   |     All, Pending, Processed,      |
|                                   |     Approved, Rejected, Error or  |
|                                   |     Cancelled                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the number of records to   |
|                                   | display from the Show records     |
|                                   | drop down list (bottom left       |
|                                   | corner of the screen)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | go to a different page by         |
|                                   | selecting either:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   First, Previous, Next or Last |
|                                   |     options, or                   |
|                                   | -   the relevant page number      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Back to Search to return   |
|                                   | to the New user request search    |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must select the  |
|                                   | new user request hyperlink in the |
|                                   | Request ID column to display a    |
|                                   | specific request record’s         |
|                                   | details:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Request ID                    |
|                                   | -   User ID                       |
|                                   | -   Family name                   |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Primary phone number          |
|                                   | -   Secondary phone number        |
|                                   | -   Email address                 |
|                                   | -   Service details               |
|                                   | -   Access level                  |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 10.                    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 10                                | New user requests menu options +  |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | There are different processes in  |
|                                   | place depending on the new user   |
|                                   | request’s status. New user        |
|                                   | requests with:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   either the Pending, Processed |
|                                   |     or Error status in ACSP means |
|                                   |     the request is incomplete and |
|                                   |     requires action (i.e. manual  |
|                                   |     intervention) from Service    |
|                                   |     Officers                      |
|                                   | -   either the Approved or        |
|                                   |     Rejected status in ACSP means |
|                                   |     the request is completed and  |
|                                   |     no further action is required |
|                                   |     from Service Officers         |
|                                   | -   with the Cancelled status in  |
|                                   |     ACSP means the request has    |
|                                   |     been cancelled due to         |
|                                   |     technical issues. See Step 21 |
|                                   |     for further details.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can choose from  |
|                                   | the following menu options:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To register or reject the new |
|                                   |     user request - go to Step 11  |
|                                   | -   To resolve a new user request |
|                                   |     with an Error status - go to  |
|                                   |     Step 20                       |
|                                   | -   To view a new user request    |
|                                   |     with a Cancelled status - go  |
|                                   |     to Step 21                    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 11                                | Registering or rejecting a new    |
|                                   | user request + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The New user request screen will  |
|                                   | display the below information for |
|                                   | the specific request:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Request ID                    |
|                                   | -   User ID                       |
|                                   | -   Family name                   |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Primary phone number          |
|                                   | -   Secondary phone number        |
|                                   | -   Email address                 |
|                                   | -   Service details               |
|                                   | -   Access level                  |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | proceed?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Register user          |
|                                   | -   go to Step 12                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, see the below Note and select |
|                                   | either                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Reject request, or            |
|                                   | -   Back to return to the New     |
|                                   |     user requests search screen   |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Selecting the Reject request  |
|                                   |     option will result in the new |
|                                   |     user request’s status in both |
|                                   |     the ACSP and the ACPP being   |
|                                   |     updated to a Rejected status  |
|                                   | -   Selecting the Back option     |
|                                   |     will result in the new user   |
|                                   |     request’s status in both the  |
|                                   |     ACSP and the ACPP remaining   |
|                                   |     as Processed and Being        |
|                                   |     Processed status respectively |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 12                                | New user request registration     |
|                                   | process - automated checks menu   |
|                                   | options + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Prior to continuing the new user  |
|                                   | request registration process,     |
|                                   | there are automated checks in     |
|                                   | place to ensure the ‘A user’ is   |
|                                   | not already registered.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | There are 3 outcomes from these   |
|                                   | automated checks:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   a 100 percent user match - go |
|                                   |     to Step 13                    |
|                                   | -   a partial user match - go to  |
|                                   |     Step 14                       |
|                                   | -   a No duplicates found match - |
|                                   |     go to Step 15                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 13                                | A 100 percent user match result + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If Service Officers selects   |
|                                   |     Back, they return to the New  |
|                                   |     user request summary page     |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   The new user request’s status |
|                                   |     in the ACSP and the ACPP will |
|                                   |     remain as Pending and Being   |
|                                   |     Processed status respectively |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the automated checks have      |
|                                   | resulted in a 100 percent user    |
|                                   | match, the New user request       |
|                                   | screen displays:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The user is already           |
|                                   |     registered. The request must  |
|                                   |     be rejected information       |
|                                   |     message                       |
|                                   | -   New user details - details    |
|                                   |     the Family name, Given name   |
|                                   |     and email address of the new  |
|                                   |     ‘A user’                      |
|                                   | -   Existing users - the table    |
|                                   |     details the matched results   |
|                                   |     i.e. displays the existing ‘A |
|                                   |     user’s’ details               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must select:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reject request                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The new user request is       |
|                                   |     rejected                      |
|                                   | -   The new user request’s status |
|                                   |     in both the ACSP and the ACPP |
|                                   |     is updated to a Rejected      |
|                                   |     status                        |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 14                                | A partial user match result +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can also     |
|                                   |     select Back to return to the  |
|                                   |     New user request summary page |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Selecting the Back option     |
|                                   |     will result in the new user   |
|                                   |     request’s status in both the  |
|                                   |     ACSP and the ACPP remaining   |
|                                   |     as Pending and Being          |
|                                   |     Processed status respectively |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the automated checks have      |
|                                   | resulted in a partial user match, |
|                                   | the New user request screen       |
|                                   | displays:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Please check the table    |
|                                   |     below for similar users. If   |
|                                   |     the user is already           |
|                                   |     registered, please reject the |
|                                   |     application information       |
|                                   |     message                       |
|                                   | -   New user details - details    |
|                                   |     the Family name, Given name   |
|                                   |     and email address of the new  |
|                                   |     ‘A user’                      |
|                                   | -   Existing users - the table    |
|                                   |     details the partial matched   |
|                                   |     results e.g. displays the     |
|                                   |     existing ‘A users’ details    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To determine if the ‘A user’ is   |
|                                   | an existing user, Service         |
|                                   | Officers must cross check the new |
|                                   | ‘A user’s’ details against all    |
|                                   | results in the Existing user      |
|                                   | details table. These checks are   |
|                                   | required to minimise the chance   |
|                                   | of creating duplicate ‘A users’   |
|                                   | IDs (‘A’ numbers).                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the new ‘A user’ an existing   |
|                                   | user?                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Reject Request         |
|                                   | -   The new user request is       |
|                                   |     rejected                      |
|                                   | -   The new user request’s status |
|                                   |     in both the ACSP and the ACPP |
|                                   |     is updated to a Rejected      |
|                                   |     status                        |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Continue registration  |
|                                   | -   The successful New user       |
|                                   |     request receipt screen will   |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 16                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 15                                | A ‘No duplicates found’ match     |
|                                   | result + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can also     |
|                                   |     select Back to return to the  |
|                                   |     New user request summary page |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Selecting the Back option     |
|                                   |     will result in the new user   |
|                                   |     request’s status in both the  |
|                                   |     ACSP and the ACPP remaining   |
|                                   |     as Pending and Being          |
|                                   |     Processed status respectively |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the automated checks have      |
|                                   | resulted in a No duplicates found |
|                                   | match, the New user details       |
|                                   | screen displays:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the No duplicates found.      |
|                                   |     Please continue with the user |
|                                   |     registration information      |
|                                   |     message                       |
|                                   | -   New user details - details    |
|                                   |     the Family name, Given name   |
|                                   |     and email address of the new  |
|                                   |     ‘A user’                      |
|                                   | -   Existing users - the table    |
|                                   |     displays the No records       |
|                                   |     available information message |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | proceed with the New user         |
|                                   | registration process?             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Continue registration  |
|                                   | -   The successful New user       |
|                                   |     request receipt screen will   |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 16                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Reject Request         |
|                                   | -   The new user request is       |
|                                   |     rejected                      |
|                                   | -   The new user request’s status |
|                                   |     in both the ACSP and the ACPP |
|                                   |     is updated to a Rejected      |
|                                   |     status                        |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 16                                | The successful New user request   |
|                                   | receipt screen + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The successful New user request   |
|                                   | receipt screen displays:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The request is being processed.   |
|                                   | Please retrieve User ID to        |
|                                   | continue processing information   |
|                                   | message                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a summary of the new user request |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Request ID                    |
|                                   | -   User ID - the ‘A user’s’ ID   |
|                                   |     is not displayed at this      |
|                                   |     stage                         |
|                                   | -   Family name                   |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Primary phone number          |
|                                   | -   Secondary phone number        |
|                                   | -   Email address                 |
|                                   | -   Service details               |
|                                   | -   Access level                  |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Status - the status is        |
|                                   |     Processing                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Retrieve User ID to    |
|                                   |     display the user ID (that is, |
|                                   |     ‘A user’s’ ID)                |
|                                   | -   arrange for the ‘A user’s’    |
|                                   |     Tivoli Access Manager (TAM)   |
|                                   |     access                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 17                                | Creation of Tivoli Access Manager |
|                                   | (TAM) access + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | IT Identity Access will need to   |
|                                   | create the Tivoli Access Manager  |
|                                   | (TAM) access for the ‘A user’ to  |
|                                   | log into the ACPP.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must email these |
|                                   | details to the delegated Service  |
|                                   | Officer responsible for           |
|                                   | submitting the TAM access. The    |
|                                   | delegated Service Officer will    |
|                                   | email IT Identity Access with the |
|                                   | below details:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The user’s personal details   |
|                                   |     (Given Name, Family Name and  |
|                                   |     User ID)                      |
|                                   | -   The required access level as  |
|                                   |     indicated in the ACSP         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Details of all new user       |
|                                   |     registrations (per service)   |
|                                   |     should be compiled into 1     |
|                                   |     spreadsheet and forwarded to  |
|                                   |     IT Identity Access section in |
|                                   |     1 email to decrease           |
|                                   |     turnaround time               |
|                                   | -   When requesting TAM access    |
|                                   |     for users, the user ID must   |
|                                   |     be specified as a capital     |
|                                   |     'A', not a lowercase 'a'. The |
|                                   |     use of the lowercase causes   |
|                                   |     access issues                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 18                                | Progressing the new user request  |
|                                   | process + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once IT Identity Access has       |
|                                   | created the TAM access, Service   |
|                                   | Officers are able to progress the |
|                                   | new user request’s approval       |
|                                   | process.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the New user request search    |
|                                   | screen, Service Officers can      |
|                                   | search for a specific new user    |
|                                   | request by selecting either:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Search by Request ID - default    |
|                                   | option                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key in the ‘Request ID’ in    |
|                                   |     the Request ID* field         |
|                                   | -   Select Search                 |
|                                   | -   The New user request search   |
|                                   |     screen will display. Note:    |
|                                   |     the details of the ‘A user’   |
|                                   |     with the organisation         |
|                                   |     administrator access who      |
|                                   |     submitted the new user        |
|                                   |     request will display          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Search by User details            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key the family name in the    |
|                                   |     Family name* field            |
|                                   | -   Key the given name in the     |
|                                   |     Given name field              |
|                                   | -   Key the phone number in the   |
|                                   |     Primary phone number field    |
|                                   |     (if known)                    |
|                                   | -   Key the email address in the  |
|                                   |     Email field (if known)        |
|                                   | -   Select Search                 |
|                                   | -   The Search results displays   |
|                                   |     in a table format             |
|                                   | -   Select the new user request   |
|                                   |     hyperlink in the Request ID   |
|                                   |     column                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete the New user             |
|                                   | registration process?             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Approve request        |
|                                   | -   The You are about to approve  |
|                                   |     this request. Please make     |
|                                   |     sure the IT Identity process  |
|                                   |     is complete before approving  |
|                                   |     information message will      |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   | -   A summary of the New user     |
|                                   |     request screen will display   |
|                                   |     prompting Service Officers to |
|                                   |     confirm prior to continuing   |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The new user request’s status |
|                                   |     in both the ACSP and the ACPP |
|                                   |     is updated to Approved        |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 19                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Back to return to the  |
|                                   |     New user request search       |
|                                   |     screen (if searched by        |
|                                   |     Request ID) or the New user   |
|                                   |     request screen (if searched   |
|                                   |     by User details)              |
|                                   | -   The new user request’s status |
|                                   |     in both the ACSP and the ACPP |
|                                   |     remains as Processing and     |
|                                   |     Being Processed respectively  |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 19                                | The completion of the New user    |
|                                   | registration process + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once the New user registration    |
|                                   | process has been completed:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the SUCCESS: The request has been |
|                                   | approved message will display     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a summary of the New user request |
|                                   | screen will display:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Request ID                    |
|                                   | -   User ID                       |
|                                   | -   Family name                   |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Primary phone number          |
|                                   | -   Secondary phone number        |
|                                   | -   Email address                 |
|                                   | -   Service details               |
|                                   | -   Access level                  |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Status - the status is Approved   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers will need to     |
|                                   | select the Go to New user request |
|                                   | search to return to the New user  |
|                                   | request search screen.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 20                                | Resolving a new user request with |
|                                   | an Error status + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Error status will appear when |
|                                   | there has been a system issue     |
|                                   | with the ACPP new user request    |
|                                   | process. Service Officers will    |
|                                   | need to resolve the error status  |
|                                   | to complete the new user request  |
|                                   | process.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the New user request search  |
|                                   | results table, select the new     |
|                                   | user request hyperlink in the     |
|                                   | Request ID column.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The New user request screen will  |
|                                   | display:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the Error. There was a problem    |
|                                   | with the request. Please escalate |
|                                   | this issue to production support  |
|                                   | error message                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a summary of the new user request |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Request ID                    |
|                                   | -   User ID                       |
|                                   | -   Family name                   |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Primary phone number          |
|                                   | -   Secondary phone number        |
|                                   | -   Email address                 |
|                                   | -   Service details               |
|                                   | -   Access level                  |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Status - the status is Error  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To resolve these requests,        |
|                                   | Service Officers must ensure the  |
|                                   | escalation process is actioned    |
|                                   | appropriately:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Complete the Aged Care Portal |
|                                   |     issues Incident form via      |
|                                   |     mySupport                     |
|                                   | -   Once ICT has advised the      |
|                                   |     error has been fixed, go to   |
|                                   |     Step 7                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 21                                | Viewing a new user request with a |
|                                   | Cancelled status + Read more ...  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Cancelled status will display |
|                                   | when ICT have:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   completed their               |
|                                   |     investigation, and            |
|                                   | -   advised the new user request  |
|                                   |     has been cancelled due to     |
|                                   |     technical issues              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers will need to     |
|                                   | advise the ‘A user’ with          |
|                                   | organisation administrator access |
|                                   | they will need to submit another  |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the New user request search  |
|                                   | results table, select the new     |
|                                   | user request hyperlink in the     |
|                                   | Request ID column.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The New user request screen will  |
|                                   | display:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the Error. The request has been   |
|                                   | cancelled due to technical        |
|                                   | issues. Please contact the        |
|                                   | provider to submit another        |
|                                   | request error message             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a summary of the new user request |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Request ID                    |
|                                   | -   User ID                       |
|                                   | -   Family name                   |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Primary phone number          |
|                                   | -   Secondary phone number        |
|                                   | -   Email address                 |
|                                   | -   Service details               |
|                                   | -   Access level                  |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Status - the status is        |
|                                   |     Cancelled                     |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to search for a care recipient (Service in Context)

| Step                              | Action                            |
