| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: all home and flexible care  |
|                                   | claims can be approved in either  |
|                                   | ACSP or Aged Care Management      |
|                                   | Payment System (ACMPS). The       |
|                                   | processing of home care events    |
|                                   | can also occur in either ACSP or  |
|                                   | ACMPS. The processing of          |
|                                   | residential care events and       |
|                                   | claims must continue to occur in  |
|                                   | the System for the Payment of     |
|                                   | Aged Residential Care (SPARC).    |
|                                   | This ensures the correct          |
|                                   | processing of aged care subsidies |
|                                   | and supplements for all care      |
|                                   | types. Service Officers can also  |
|                                   | use ACSP to search for services   |
|                                   | within all care types.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following menu    |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care recipient search screen      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen - go to   |

|                                   |     3                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Event search screen               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 5                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen - go to Step |
|                                   |     6                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care recipients’ itemised         |
|                                   | entitlements                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 7                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen - go to Step |
|                                   |     8                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care recipients’ itemised         |
|                                   | payments                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 9                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen - go to Step |
|                                   |     10                            |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care recipient search via the     |

|                                   | ...                               |

|                                   |     screen displays               |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | -   on the ACSP Service in        |
|                                   |     Context home page select Care |
|                                   |     recipient search under the    |
|                                   |     Quick links navigation bar    |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient search     |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Using the Care recipient search   |

|                                   | option:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Date from* field - date range |
|                                   |     must be within 90 days of the |
|                                   |     Date to* field                |
|                                   | -   Date to* field - date range   |
|                                   |     must be within 90 days of the |
|                                   |     Date from* field              |
|                                   | -   Service – displays the name   |
|                                   |     of the service in context     |
|                                   | -   Channel - defaults to ‘Select |
|                                   |     all’. Service Officers can    |
|                                   |     select either Select all,     |
|                                   |     Services Australia or Portal  |
|                                   | -   Event type                    |
|                                   | -   Event status                  |
|                                   | -   Care recipient ID             |
|                                   | -   select Search button to       |
|                                   |     display the event details     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Search by Event ID. To select     |
|                                   | this option, Service Officers     |
|                                   | must select the Event ID option   |
|                                   | from the drop down list:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service - defaults to the     |
|                                   |     current service. Users can    |
|                                   |     select a different service    |
|                                   |     from the drop down list       |
|                                   | -   Type the event ID in the      |
|                                   |     Event ID* field               |
|                                   | -   Select Search button to       |
|                                   |     display the event details     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Search by Additional days. To     |
|                                   | select this option, Service       |
|                                   | Officers must select the          |
|                                   | Additional days option from the   |
|                                   | drop down list:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Date from* field              |
|                                   | -   Date to* field                |
|                                   | -   Action field                  |
|                                   | -   Care recipient ID field       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Search button to display   |
|                                   | the event details.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

|                                   | relevant event type to view       |

|                                   | select the hyperlinked Status ID  |
|                                   | to display individual event's     |
|                                   | details                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Supplements tab - this tab is     |
|                                   | only applicable to home and       |
|                                   | residential care services. Select |
|                                   | the relevant supplement type to   |
|                                   | view details. Select the Register |
|                                   | button under the relevant         |
|                                   | supplement type to register new   |
|                                   | supplement or select the          |

|                                   | the individual supplement’s       |
|                                   | details                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Additional days - this tab is     |
|                                   | only applicable to transition     |
|                                   | care services. Select the tab to  |
|                                   | process transition care extension |
|                                   | requests                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Commonwealth amount tab - this    |
|                                   | tab is only applicable to home    |
|                                   | care services. Select the tab to  |
|                                   | display CW Unspent amounts -      |

|                                   | amount on departure, Invoice      |
|                                   | amount and Home care account. Go  |

|                                   | Home to return to the ACSP        |
|                                   | Service in Context home page      |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to search for a care recipient – (Care Recipient in Context (CRiC))

Table 10

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: all home and flexible care  |
|                                   | claims can be approved in either  |
|                                   | ACSP or Aged Care Management      |
|                                   | Payment System (ACMPS). The       |
|                                   | processing of home care events    |
|                                   | can also occur in either ACSP or  |
|                                   | ACMPS. The processing of          |
|                                   | residential care events and       |
|                                   | claims must continue to occur in  |
|                                   | the System for the Payment of     |
|                                   | Aged Residential Care (SPARC).    |
|                                   | This ensures the correct          |
|                                   | processing of aged care subsidies |
|                                   | and supplements for all care      |
|                                   | types. Service Officers can also  |
|                                   | use ACSP to search for services   |
|                                   | within all care types.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following menu    |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Care recipient search         |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 2         |
|                                   | -   Care recipient summary        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 4         |
|                                   | -   Care recipient details        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 5         |
|                                   | -   Care recipient journey        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 6         |
|                                   | -   Approval details screen - go  |
|                                   |     to Step 7                     |
|                                   | -   Medicare card details         |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 8         |
|                                   | -   Event summary screen - go to  |
|                                   |     Step 9                        |
|                                   | -   Payments menu tab - go to     |
|                                   |     Step 10                       |

| 3                                 | Using the Care recipient search   |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Officers may need to  |
|                                   |     refine their search results   |
|                                   |     if the 'Your search matched X |
|                                   |     care recipients. Only 200     |
|                                   |     care recipients are displayed |
|                                   |     in care recipient ID order    |
|                                   |     below. Please refine your     |
|                                   |     search criteria if needed'    |
|                                   |     information message displays  |
|                                   |     and they cannot locate the    |
|                                   |     relevant care recipient from  |
|                                   |     the search results            |
|                                   | -   All fields are optional       |
|                                   |     unless marked with an         |
|                                   |     asterisk                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use the Care recipient search     |
|                                   | screen to search for a care       |
|                                   | recipient by:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Care recipient details        |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Getaway (ACG) ID    |
|                                   | -   Centrelink ID                 |
|                                   | -   Department of Veterans’       |
|                                   |     Affairs (DVA) ID              |
|                                   | -   Recent searches               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Search by Care recipient       |
|                                   | details + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Care recipient details in  |
|                                   | the Search by* field              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | complete the below fields:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Care recipient ID* - if       |
|                                   |     searching by Care recipient   |
|                                   |     ID, the mandatory asterisk    |
|                                   |     against the Family name field |
|                                   |     disappears                    |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Family name* - if searching   |
|                                   |     by Family name, the mandatory |
|                                   |     asterisk against the Care     |
|                                   |     recipient ID field disappears |
|                                   | -   Date of birth                 |
|                                   | -   Gender - select from the drop |
|                                   |     down list                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Search button          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient summary    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Search by Aged Care Getaway    |
|                                   | (ACG) ID + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Aged Care Getaway (ACG) ID |
|                                   | in the Search by* field           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | key the Aged Care Getaway (ACG)   |
|                                   | ID in the ACG ID* field           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Search button          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient summary    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Search by Centrelink ID + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Centrelink ID in the       |
|                                   | Search by* field                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | key the Centrelink ID in the      |
|                                   | Centrelink ID* field              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Search button          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient summary    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Search by Department of        |
|                                   | Veterans’ Affairs (DVA) ID + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Department of Veterans’    |
|                                   | Affairs (DVA) ID in the Search    |
|                                   | by* field                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | key the DVA ID in the DVA ID*     |
|                                   | field                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Search button          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient summary    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Search by Recent searches +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Care recipient ID in the Recent   |
|                                   | searches section results table    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient summary    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |

| 4                                 | Care recipient summary screen +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An alternate way to go to the     |
|                                   | Care recipient journey screen is  |
|                                   | by using the Main menu (Hamburger |
|                                   | Button). Select Care recipient    |
|                                   | journey, under the Care recipient |
|                                   | section, from the Main menu       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   type in a keyword in the      |

|                                   |     description of the various    |
|                                   |     care types                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Care recipient summary screen |
|                                   | displays the following:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care Recipient banner - displays  |
|                                   | the care recipient’s name, IDs,   |
|                                   | Date of Birth, Record type and    |
|                                   | Type of care status               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care recipient service entries -  |
|                                   | displays the information in a     |
|                                   | table format                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service NAPS ID - select the  |
|                                   |     relevant hyperlinked Service  |
|                                   |     NAPS ID and the ACSP Service  |
|                                   |     in Context home page displays |
|                                   | -   Service RACS ID - select the  |
|                                   |     relevant hyperlinked Service  |
|                                   |     NAPS ID and the ACSP Service  |
|                                   |     in Context home page displays |
|                                   | -   Service name                  |
|                                   | -   Care type                     |
|                                   | -   Entry date                    |
|                                   | -   Departure date                |
|                                   | -   Departure reason              |
|                                   | -   Entry status - select the     |
|                                   |     relevant hyperlinked Entry    |
|                                   |     status record and the         |
|                                   |     specific Entry event details  |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   | -   Care recipient journey -      |
|                                   |     select the relevant           |
|                                   |     hyperlinked Care recipient    |
|                                   |     journey record and the Care   |
|                                   |     recipient journey screen      |
|                                   |     displays. Go to Step 6 for    |
|                                   |     information about this        |
|                                   |     screen.                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Recent approval details section - |
|                                   | displays the care recipient’s     |
|                                   | last 5 most recent approval       |
|                                   | details. Select the View all      |
|                                   | button to display the Approval    |
|                                   | summary screen. Go to Step 7 for  |
|                                   | information about this screen     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Recent letters section - this is  |
|                                   | a placeholder and the No records  |
|                                   | available information message     |
|                                   | will display                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | By hovering the mouse pointer     |
|                                   | over the Care recipient tab until |
|                                   | the pop up window displays,       |
|                                   | Service Officers can select from  |
|                                   | the following screens:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Care recipient details        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 5         |
|                                   | -   Care recipient journey        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 6         |
|                                   | -   Approval details screen - go  |
|                                   |     to Step 7                     |
|                                   | -   Medicare card details         |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 8         |
|                                   | -   Event summary screen - go to  |
|                                   |     Step 9                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

|                                   |     recipients                    |

|                                   |     relevant claim year           |

|                                   |     drop down list to select the  |
|                                   |     relevant claim month          |

|                                   |     drop down list to select the  |
|                                   |     relevant claim year           |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | services                          |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     by section Note: Select Clear |

|                                   |     this will present the         |

|                                   |     (original) state and then     |

|                                   |     information that is available |

| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: all home and flexible care  |
|                                   | claims can be approved in either  |
|                                   | ACSP or Aged Care Management      |
|                                   | Payment System (ACMPS). The       |
|                                   | processing of home care events    |
|                                   | can also occur in either ACSP or  |
|                                   | ACMPS. The processing of          |
|                                   | residential care events and       |
|                                   | claims must continue to occur in  |
|                                   | the System for the Payment of     |
|                                   | Aged Residential Care (SPARC).    |
|                                   | This ensures the correct          |
|                                   | processing of aged care subsidies |
|                                   | and supplements for all care      |
|                                   | types. Service Officers can also  |
|                                   | use ACSP to search for services   |
|                                   | within all care types.            |

|                                   | assessment information. All       |

|                                   | screen.                           |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal for home care purposes - (Service in Context)

Table 12

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can use ACSP to  |
|                                   | register invoice amounts, report  |
|                                   | Commonwealth (CW) unspent amounts |
|                                   | and view a care recipient’s home  |
|                                   | care account for home care        |
|                                   | purposes only. These events are   |
|                                   | specific to home care services.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following menu    |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | CW Unspent amounts - Report and   |
|                                   | Opt in                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 2                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen - go to Step |
|                                   |     3                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | CW Unspent amount on departure -  |
|                                   | go to Step 6                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Invoice amount - go to Step 11    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Home care account                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 19                       |
|                                   | -   Using the screen - go to Step |
|                                   |     20                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Going to the CW Unspent amounts - |
|                                   | Report and Opt in screen + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the CW Unspent amounts -    |
|                                   | Report and Opt in screen is       |
|                                   | available when the service in     |
|                                   | context’s current claim is the    |
|                                   | September 2021 claim onwards.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the CW Unspent amounts -    |
|                                   | Report and Opt in screen by:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log into Aged Care Staff Portal   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Welcome to the Aged Care      |
|                                   | Staff Portal home page screen     |
|                                   | (the ACSP home page) displays     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   select Service Search         |
|                                   | -   the Service Search screen     |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   | -   key the service’s details     |
|                                   | -   select Search                 |
|                                   | -   select the hyperlinked        |
|                                   |     Service NAPS ID in the search |
|                                   |     results table                 |
|                                   | -   the ACSP Service in Context   |
|                                   |     home page displays            |
|                                   | -   select Care recipient search  |
|                                   |     (service) under the Service   |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient search     |
|                                   |     (service) screen displays     |
|                                   | -   key the care recipient’s      |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   select Search                 |

|                                   |     entries screen displays       |

|                                   | screen displays                   |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | -   Amount*                       |
|                                   | -   Opt in* - only available      |
|                                   |     during the opt-in period      |
|                                   |     (that is, 1 September 2021 to |
|                                   |     28 February 2022 inclusive)   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete the Register reported    |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amount       |
|                                   | process?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The successful recipient      |
|                                   |     message will display          |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel to cancel the   |
|                                   |     Register reported             |
|                                   |     Commonwealth unspent amount   |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   | -   The Cancel message will       |
|                                   |     display asking Service        |
|                                   |     Officers to select Yes or No  |
|                                   |     to cancel the event           |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Using the View reported           |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amount       |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |

|                                   | -   CW Unspent amount on          |
|                                   |     departure - go to Step 6      |
|                                   | -   Invoice amount - go to Step   |
|                                   |     11                            |
|                                   | -   Home care account - go to     |
|                                   |     Step 19                       |

| 5                                 | Updating or deleting a reported   |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amount +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Update reported Commonwealth  |
|                                   | unspent amount screen:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   displays for home care        |
|                                   |     services only                 |
|                                   | -   is available when the service |
|                                   |     in context’s current claim is |
|                                   |     the September 2021 claim      |
|                                   |     onwards                       |
|                                   | -   displays the details of an    |
|                                   |     individual reported           |
|                                   |     Commonwealth (CW) unspent     |
|                                   |     amount                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the Update reported        |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amount       |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | complete the following fields:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Amount*                       |
|                                   | -   Opt in - only available       |
|                                   |     during the opt-in period      |
|                                   |     (that is, 1 September 2021 to |
|                                   |     28 February 2022 inclusive)   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select either                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Submit to complete the Update |
|                                   |     reported Commonwealth unspent |
|                                   |     amount process                |
|                                   | -   Cancel and return to the View |
|                                   |     reported Commonwealth unspent |
|                                   |     amount screen                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Delete a Reported Commonwealth |
|                                   | unspent amount                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select in the Delete? pop up      |
|                                   | notification either:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes to complete the deletion  |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   | -   Cancel and return to the View |
|                                   |     reported Commonwealth unspent |
|                                   |     amount screen                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

| 7                                 | Register individual CW Unspent    |
|                                   | amount on departure + Read more   |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The screen name may be        |
|                                   |     different depending on the    |
|                                   |     service in context’s current  |
|                                   |     claim month                   |
|                                   | -   The Commonwealth unspent      |
|                                   |     amount on departure summary   |
|                                   |     screen is available when the  |
|                                   |     service in context’s current  |
|                                   |     claim is the September 2021   |
|                                   |     claim onwards                 |
|                                   | -   The CW Unspent Amount screen  |
|                                   |     is available when the service |
|                                   |     in context’s current claim is |
|                                   |     prior to the September 2021   |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   | -   All fields are optional       |
|                                   |     unless marked with an         |
|                                   |     asterisk                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Register Commonwealth unspent  |
|                                   | amount on departure:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log into Aged Care Staff Portal   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Welcome to the Aged Care      |
|                                   | Staff Portal home page screen     |
|                                   | (the ACSP home page) displays     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   select Service Search         |
|                                   | -   the Service Search screen     |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   | -   key the service’s details     |
|                                   | -   select Search                 |
|                                   | -   select the hyperlinked        |
|                                   |     Service NAPS ID in the search |
|                                   |     results table                 |
|                                   | -   the ACSP Service in Context   |
|                                   |     home page displays            |
|                                   | -   select Care recipient search  |
|                                   |     (service) under the Service   |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient search     |
|                                   |     (service) screen displays     |
|                                   | -   key the care recipient’s      |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   select Search                 |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient service    |
|                                   |     entries screen displays       |
|                                   | -   select Go to current profile  |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient profile    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   | -   select the Commonwealth       |
|                                   |     amount tab                    |
|                                   | -   hover the mouse pointer over  |
|                                   |     the Commonwealth amount menu  |
|                                   |     tab                           |
|                                   | -   a pop up window displays      |
|                                   | -   select CW Unspent amount on   |
|                                   |     departure                     |
|                                   | -   the Commonwealth unspent      |
|                                   |     amount on departure summary   |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Commonwealth unspent       |
|                                   | amount on departure summary       |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Register Commonwealth  |
|                                   | unspent amount on departure       |
|                                   | button                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Register Commonwealth     |
|                                   |     unspent amount on departure   |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | key the departure date in the     |
|                                   | Departure date field              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | key the amount in the             |
|                                   | Commonwealth portion of unspent   |
|                                   | home care amount on departure*    |
|                                   | field                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete the Register             |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amount on    |
|                                   | departure event process?          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, select Submit to         |
|                                   |     complete the Register         |
|                                   |     Commonwealth unspent amount   |
|                                   |     on departure event process    |
|                                   | -   No, select Cancel to cancel   |
|                                   |     the Commonwealth unspent      |
|                                   |     amounts event and return to   |
|                                   |     the Commonwealth unspent      |
|                                   |     amount summary screen         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can update       |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amounts on   |
|                                   | departure. Go to Step 8.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

| 10                                | Registering Bulk reporting        |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amounts +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Bulk reporting            |
|                                   |     Commonwealth unspent amounts  |
|                                   |     screen is available when the  |
|                                   |     service in context’s current  |
|                                   |     claim is the September 2021   |
|                                   |     claim onwards                 |
|                                   | -   An error message will display |
|                                   |     if the Amount* field has not  |
|                                   |     been completed for all care   |
|                                   |     recipients. Service Officers  |
|                                   |     must either enter the missing |
|                                   |     amounts or set all the care   |
|                                   |     recipients’ Amount* field to  |
|                                   |     zero dollars ($0) by          |
|                                   |     selecting Set to 0.0          |
|                                   | -   If the event has been         |
|                                   |     submitted successfully, a     |
|                                   |     successful receipt message    |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   | -   All fields are optional       |
|                                   |     unless marked with an         |
|                                   |     asterisk                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must carefully   |
|                                   | review each care recipient’s      |
|                                   | information before submitting the |
|                                   | Bulk reporting Commonwealth       |
|                                   | unspent amounts events.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Bulk reporting Commonwealth   |
|                                   | unspent amounts screen displays   |
|                                   | the following information in a    |
|                                   | table format:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care recipient                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ID                            |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Family name                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amount       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Amount                        |
|                                   | -   Opt in - only available       |
|                                   |     during the opt-in period      |
|                                   |     (that is, 1 September 2021 to |
|                                   |     28 February 2022 inclusive)   |
|                                   | -   Submission Status             |
|                                   | -   Event Status                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To register Bulk reporting        |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amounts,     |
|                                   | complete:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Amount* field             |
|                                   | -   the Opt in field - only       |
|                                   |     available during the opt-in   |
|                                   |     period (that is, 1 September  |
|                                   |     2021 to 28 February 2022      |
|                                   |     inclusive)                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete registering the Bulk     |
|                                   | reporting Commonwealth unspent    |
|                                   | amounts process?                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The successful recipient      |
|                                   |     message will display          |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No                                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel to cancel the   |
|                                   |     Bulk reporting Commonwealth   |
|                                   |     unspent amounts process       |
|                                   | -   The Cancel message will       |
|                                   |     display asking Service        |
|                                   |     Officers to select Yes or No  |
|                                   |     to cancel the event           |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | type in a keyword in the Search   |
|                                   | bar to search for all records     |
|                                   | that contain the keyword          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | filter the records by the         |
|                                   | Submission Status to narrow the   |
|                                   | records                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Delete All to delete all   |
|                                   | Bulk reporting Commonwealth       |
|                                   | unspent amounts records           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Import CSV to perform a    |
|                                   | bulk import of Bulk reporting     |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amounts from |
|                                   | a CSV file                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Export CSV to export all   |
|                                   | the content of the Bulk reporting |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amounts      |
|                                   | screen into a CSV file            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | set all the care recipients’      |
|                                   | Amount* field to zero dollars     |
|                                   | ($0) by selecting Set to 0.0      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Check all submitted Opt in |
|                                   | to opt in all care recipients for |
|                                   | the current claim month           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the number of records to   |
|                                   | display from the Show records     |
|                                   | drop down list (bottom left       |
|                                   | corner of the screen)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Go to the current claim to |
|                                   | display the Current claim screen  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Close to return to the     |
|                                   | ACSP Service in Context home page |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | go to a different page by         |
|                                   | selecting either the:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   First, Previous, Next or Last |
|                                   |     options, or                   |
|                                   | -   the relevant page number      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

|                                   | -   Submitted by                  |

|                                   | -   Claim month                   |
|                                   | -   Amount                        |
|                                   | -   Paid amount                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can select:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Event history to display the      |
|                                   | history of an individual Invoice  |
|                                   | amount event                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Close to return to the Invoice    |
|                                   | amount screen                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update to display the Update      |
|                                   | invoice amount screen. Go to Step |
|                                   | 16                                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Delete to delete an Invoice       |
|                                   | amount                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Delete? pop up            |
|                                   |     notification will display     |
|                                   |     asking Service Officers to    |
|                                   |     select Yes or No to cancel    |
|                                   |     the event                     |
|                                   | -   Select Yes and the individual |
|                                   |     Invoice amount entry is       |
|                                   |     deleted                       |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 15                                | The Register invoice amount       |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Register invoice amount       |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   displays for home care        |
|                                   |     services only                 |
|                                   | -   is available when the service |
|                                   |     in context’s current claim is |
|                                   |     the September 2021 claim      |
|                                   |     onwards                       |
|                                   | -   displays Care Recipient       |
|                                   |     banner - displays the care    |
|                                   |     recipient’s name, IDs, Date   |
|                                   |     of Birth, Record type and     |
|                                   |     Type of care status           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claim month field defaults to |
|                                   | the service the service in        |
|                                   | context’s current claim month     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Invoice amounts cannot be updated |
|                                   | once the claim has been           |
|                                   | finalised. If a previous invoice  |
|                                   | amount has been incorrectly       |
|                                   | entered, Service Officers can use |
|                                   | the Register invoice amount       |
|                                   | screen to reflect the adjustment. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For example - scenario 1          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the December 2022 invoice     |
|                                   |     amount was originally $60,000 |
|                                   | -   the home care service         |
|                                   |     determined in June 2023 that  |
|                                   |     the December 2022 invoice     |
|                                   |     amount should have been       |
|                                   |     $100,000                      |
|                                   | -   the June 2023 invoice amount  |
|                                   |     has been calculated as        |
|                                   |     $100,000                      |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can use the  |
|                                   |     Register invoice amount       |
|                                   |     screen to add the additional  |
|                                   |     $40,000 as part of the        |
|                                   |     current claim month’s invoice |
|                                   |     amount by entering an invoice |
|                                   |     amount of $140,000 for June   |
|                                   |     2023                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For example - scenario 2          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the March 2023 invoice amount |
|                                   |     was originally $140,000       |
|                                   | -   the home care service         |
|                                   |     determined in July 2023 that  |
|                                   |     the March 2023 invoice amount |
|                                   |     should have been $100,000     |
|                                   | -   the July 2023 invoice amount  |
|                                   |     has been calculated as        |
|                                   |     $100,000                      |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can use the  |
|                                   |     Register invoice amount       |
|                                   |     screen to reduce the current  |
|                                   |     claim month’s invoice amount  |
|                                   |     by $40,000 by entering an     |
|                                   |     invoice amount of $60,000 for |
|                                   |     July 2023                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Register invoice amount,       |
|                                   | complete the Amount* field.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete registering the Register |
|                                   | invoice amount?                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The successful recipient      |
|                                   |     message will display          |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel to cancel the   |
|                                   |     Register invoice amount       |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   | -   The Cancel message will       |
|                                   |     display asking Service        |
|                                   |     Officers to select Yes or No  |
|                                   |     to cancel the event           |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
