Registering events in the Aged Care Staff Portal (Service in Context)

Table 13

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Register an event in the Aged     |
|                                   | Care Staff Portal (ACSP) + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: all home and flexible care  |
|                                   | claims can be approved in either  |
|                                   | ACSP or Aged Care Management      |
|                                   | Payment System (ACMPS). The       |
|                                   | processing of home care events    |
|                                   | can also occur in either ACSP or  |
|                                   | ACMPS. The processing of          |
|                                   | residential care events and       |
|                                   | claims must continue to occur in  |
|                                   | the System for the Payment of     |
|                                   | Aged Residential Care (SPARC).    |
|                                   | This ensures the correct          |
|                                   | processing of aged care subsidies |
|                                   | and supplements for all care      |
|                                   | types. Service Officers can also  |
|                                   | use ACSP to search for services   |
|                                   | within all care types.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the ACSP:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Register an entry event - go  |
|                                   |     to Step 2                     |
|                                   | -   Register a leave event - go   |
|                                   |     to Step 7                     |
|                                   | -   Register a departure event -  |
|                                   |     go to Step 8                  |
|                                   | -   Register care setting days -  |
|                                   |     go to Step 10                 |
|                                   | -   Register bulk events - go to  |
|                                   |     Step 12                       |
|                                   | -   Register Additional days - go |
|                                   |     to Step 14                    |
|                                   | -   Update an existing event - go |
|                                   |     to Step 15                    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Register an entry event + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select an entry date less     |
|                                   |     than 2 years before (or equal |
|                                   |     to) the current date          |
|                                   | -   This step is applicable to    |
|                                   |     all care types except         |
|                                   |     residential care              |
|                                   | -   All fields are mandatory      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Entry events are registered in an |
|                                   | individual care recipient         |
|                                   | profile:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Circumstances tab      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Entry                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Entry summary screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Register entry button  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Register entry screen     |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Register entry screen,     |
|                                   | complete:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Type of care* field               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the relevant care type |
|                                   |     from the drop-down field      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Hospital admission date* field -  |
|                                   | this is only applicable for       |
|                                   | transition care recipients        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Entry date* field                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Level of care* field - applicable |
|                                   | for home care recipients only     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Carer status* field - applicable  |
|                                   | for home care recipients only     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Functional capacity score (MBI)   |
|                                   | on entry* field - applicable for  |
|                                   | home care recipients only         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the Register entry event       |
|                                   | process complete?                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 3                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel                 |
|                                   | -   A message displays asking to  |
|                                   |     select Yes or No to cancel    |
|                                   |     the process                   |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | The entry event’s status + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An entry event is successful when |
|                                   | the status is Accepted.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the entry event successful?   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The entry event status is a   |
|                                   |     Held status                   |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 4                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Held entry events + Read more ... |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Entry events with a Held status   |
|                                   | will not be processed as part of  |
|                                   | the current claim’s finalisation  |
|                                   | process and may result in over    |
|                                   | occupancy issues.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These entry events are due to     |
|                                   | either a:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   known timing issue with over  |
|                                   |     lapping periods of care, or   |
|                                   | -   genuine over lapping period   |
|                                   |     of care                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A known timing issue with         |
|                                   | overlapping periods of care is    |
|                                   | where the care recipient has      |
|                                   | entered in to care of the new     |
|                                   | aged care service but a departure |
|                                   | event has not be submitted by the |
|                                   | previous aged care service.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These entry events are resolved   |
|                                   | when Services Australia has       |
|                                   | received the departure event from |
|                                   | the previous aged care service.   |
|                                   | No manual intervention is         |
|                                   | required from Service Officers.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the held entry event due to a  |
|                                   | known timing issue?               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   No manual intervention is     |
|                                   |     required from Service         |
|                                   |     Officers                      |
|                                   | -   The entry event will be       |
|                                   |     resolved when Services        |
|                                   |     Australia has received the    |
|                                   |     departure event from the      |
|                                   |     previous aged care service    |
|                                   | -   Process is complete           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 5                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Remediating genuine overlapping   |
|                                   | entry and departure dates between |
|                                   | 2 services + Read more ...        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A genuine over lapping period of  |
|                                   | care is where the care recipient  |
|                                   | has entered in to care of the new |
|                                   | aged care service and the entry   |
|                                   | date overlaps with the departure  |
|                                   | event submitted by the previous   |
|                                   | aged care service.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For held entry events due to a    |
|                                   | genuine over lapping period of    |
|                                   | care, Service Officers will need  |
|                                   | to manually remediate these cases |
|                                   | to ensure the entry event is      |
|                                   | accepted.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To remediate the overlap, Service |
|                                   | Officers will need to:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   identify the ‘source’ service |
|                                   |     (that is, identify the        |
|                                   |     service the care recipient    |
|                                   |     would have been entered into  |
|                                   |     first)                        |
|                                   | -   map out the entry and         |
|                                   |     departure dates for each      |
|                                   |     service and put them into the |
|                                   |     correct date order            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must contact the |
|                                   | service they are processing the   |
|                                   | event for to confirm the correct  |
|                                   | entry or departure date.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the Service Officers          |
|                                   | successfully contacted the        |
|                                   | service to confirm the correct    |
|                                   | entry or departure dates?         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Update the events’ dates to   |
|                                   |     ‘remove the overlap’ in dates |
|                                   | -   See Step 15 for the process   |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 6                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Officers are not to   |
|                                   |     process the entry or          |
|                                   |     departure events              |
|                                   | -   See Step 3 in the Care        |
|                                   |     recipient notes in ACMPS      |
|                                   |     table in Manage aged care     |
|                                   |     recipient details to create a |
|                                   |     care recipient note advising  |
|                                   |     an attempt to contact the     |
|                                   |     service was unsuccessful and  |
|                                   |     no action has been taken      |
|                                   | -   See Step 2 in the Maintain    |
|                                   |     payment statements notes in   |
|                                   |     ACMPS table in Payment        |
|                                   |     statements for aged care      |
|                                   |     services to create a payment  |
|                                   |     statement note in ACMPS.      |
|                                   |     Suggested wording to use is   |
|                                   |     “[CR number and name] unable  |
|                                   |     to process entry/departure    |
|                                   |     due to overlap in dates with  |
|                                   |     another service. Please       |
|                                   |     reclaim.”                     |
|                                   | -   Re-finalise the claim. See    |
|                                   |     Step 5 in Table 6 for the     |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Add a care recipient note for     |
|                                   | successful contacts and           |
|                                   | re-finalise the claim + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When the updates to the events’   |
|                                   | dates have been completed,        |
|                                   | Service Officers must:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Step 3 in the Care recipient  |
|                                   | notes in ACMPS table in Manage    |
|                                   | aged care recipient details to    |
|                                   | create a care recipient note. The |
|                                   | care recipient note must include  |
|                                   | the full name and contact number  |
|                                   | of service contact the Service    |
|                                   | Officer had spoken to and         |
|                                   | confirmation of action undertaken |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | re-finalise the claim             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See Table 6 Step 5 for the    |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Registering a leave event + Read  |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This step is only applicable to   |
|                                   | home care and short-term          |
|                                   | restorative care services         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For flexible care services,       |
|                                   | select a start date less than 2   |
|                                   | years before (or equal to) the    |
|                                   | current date                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For home care leave events that   |
|                                   | occurred on or after 1 September  |
|                                   | 2021 onwards, select a date that  |
|                                   | is less than:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   2 years before (or equal to)  |
|                                   |     the current date for care     |
|                                   |     recipients who are still in   |
|                                   |     the service’s care            |
|                                   | -   70 days before (or equal to)  |
|                                   |     the current date for care     |
|                                   |     recipients who have departed  |
|                                   |     from the service              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For home care leave events that   |
|                                   | occurred prior to 1 September     |
|                                   | 2021:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select a date that is less    |
|                                   |     than 2 years before (or equal |
|                                   |     to) the current date          |
|                                   | -   this applies for all current  |
|                                   |     and departed care recipients  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the event submits              |
|                                   | successfully, a successful        |
|                                   | message displays                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Register a leave event in an      |
|                                   | individual care recipient         |
|                                   | profile:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Circumstances tab      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Leave                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Leave summary screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Register leave button  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Register leave screen     |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select an option from the Leave   |
|                                   | type* drop down list              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | type the start date in the Leave  |
|                                   | start date* field                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | type the end date in the Leave    |
|                                   | end date field                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the Register leave event       |
|                                   | complete?                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, select Submit                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel                 |
|                                   | -   A message displays asking to  |
|                                   |     select Yes or No to cancel    |
|                                   |     the event                     |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The Register leave event      |
|                                   |     process has been cancelled    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel                 |
|                                   | -   A message displays asking to  |
|                                   |     select Yes or No to cancel    |
|                                   |     the process                   |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The Register additional       |
|                                   |     transition care days process  |
|                                   |     has been cancelled            |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |

| 15                                | Updating an existing event + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This step is applicable to home   |
|                                   | care and flexible care services   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For flexible care services:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select a start date less than |
|                                   |     2 years before (or equal to)  |
|                                   |     the current date when         |
|                                   |     updating an existing event    |
|                                   | -   To update care setting days,  |
|                                   |     Service Officers must first   |
|                                   |     delete the original care      |
|                                   |     setting days event and then   |
|                                   |     create a new care setting day |
|                                   |     event                         |
|                                   | -   To register care setting days |
|                                   |     (create a new care setting    |
|                                   |     day event), go to Step 10     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For home care events that         |
|                                   | occurred on or after 1 September  |
|                                   | 2021 onwards, select a date that  |
|                                   | is less than:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   2 years before (or equal to)  |
|                                   |     the current date for care     |
|                                   |     recipients who are still in   |
|                                   |     the service’s care            |
|                                   | -   70 days before (or equal to)  |
|                                   |     the current date for care     |
|                                   |     recipients who have departed  |
|                                   |     from the service’s care       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For home care events that         |
|                                   | occurred prior to 1 September     |
|                                   | 2021:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select a date that is less    |
|                                   |     than 2 years before (or equal |
|                                   |     to) the current date          |
|                                   | -   this applies for all current  |
|                                   |     and departed care recipients  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the event submits              |
|                                   | successfully, a successful        |
|                                   | message displays                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update or delete an event in the  |
|                                   | individual event’s details screen |
|                                   | (the event history):              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Update button and  |
|                                   |     add the relevant details, or  |
|                                   | -   select the Delete button      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the update (or deletion)       |
|                                   | complete?                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Submit to complete the |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel                 |
|                                   | -   A message displays asking to  |
|                                   |     select Yes or No to cancel    |
|                                   |     the update (or deletion)      |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
